News Brief Two

Zhu Mao Capture Various Counties in Southern Jiangxi 74

▲They have crossed Nankang and Dayu and invaded Guangdong.

Nanchang Correspondence: Zhu Mao recently attacked Ganzhou, but was besieged by the Peng and Yu regiments and the Zhou, Xiao, and Yang regiments of Jin's division. Zhu's bandits were unable to withstand the attack and abandoned Ganzhou on March 22. They used a small part to cause trouble in Shangyou, Suichuan, and invade Yundu and Guoji to disperse the bandit suppression forces, while the majority fled from Nankang, Dayu, and Xinfeng to the border of Nanxiong and Sannan, peeking at the East River of Guangdong. The vanguard troops have already reached the Nanxiong border area of Guangdong. It is reported that the Guangdong army's Dai brigade and Wu regiment have opened to Nanxiong and Xinghua areas in northern Guangdong to carry out interception. However, when Zhu Mao fled south, there were no troops stationed on the border between Jiangxi and Guangdong. The counties they passed through suffered unbearable devastation. According to a telegram from the Nankang Court to the Higher Court, the county seat of Nankang was captured by Zhu's bandits last month, and the county government, court, party headquarters, and all public buildings were burned down by the communists, and the prisoners escaped completely. The county seat of Dayu was also lost at noon, the prisons were overthrown and the government was destroyed, and it was chaotic. The county magistrate of Dayu, Zhu Rulin, telegraphed to the province yesterday, saying that Jin's division had sent a team to chase them, and Xunwu, because it borders Fujian and Guangdong provinces, has always been a den of bandits. The scattered bandits in the county took the opportunity to respond and captured the county seat. The county magistrate, Hu Zehuan, escaped in advance. Later, the acting county magistrate, Hu Mengchun, led the Jingwei team to counterattack and killed the bandit leaders Liu Jiangxia and Zou Caichen on the spot, and beheaded them for public display, and regained the county seat. Other counties such as Xinfeng and Longnan are also extremely panicked and in a dangerous situation. The current situation is not yet known. As for Yichun in western Jiangxi, it was attacked by Peng Dehuai on March 24, and the county government, Qingxiang Bureau, and Finance Bureau were all burned down. The Civil Affairs Department received a telegram from the county magistrate of the county, Cai Shu, saying that Wang's regiment of Deng Yunshan's brigade arrived on the morning of the 26th, and the bandits were repelled and the county seat was recovered, and order has been restored. Zhang Huizan, the commander-in-chief of bandit suppression in Jiangxi Province, led the headquarters to Zhangshu a few days ago. Because the scattered bandits along the Gan River were still rampant, he temporarily stationed in Xingan. Now the communists along the river from the province to Ji'an have been completely eliminated. Zhang then advanced from Jishui and stationed in Ji'an, directing everything, and telegraphed to Chairman Lu many ways to eliminate the banditry, such as clearing the countryside, providing disaster relief, and self-defense. Chairman Lu has adopted and implemented them. As for the Security Office established by the provincial government, it was formally established today. All newly established Jingwei Regiments, Police Brigades, Qingxiang Cadre Teams, and Radio Teams are under its jurisdiction. The Provincial Qingxiang Bureau, which was established earlier, was ended at the end of last month and handed over to the Security Office for takeover. (April 1)

Three Records of the Robbery in Zhangyan Town, Jinshan 75

Songjiang Correspondence: The case of robbery and kidnapping in Zhangyan Town, Jinshan County, has been reported twice in this newspaper. I now know that the next day (2nd), the Jinshan County Government only sent a committee member to Zhangyan to investigate and ordered all pawnbrokers to seal up all the remaining clothes and jewelry and wait for discussions on how to deal with the aftermath. Shops such as Hengtai Xiang, Xiechang, and Yangguang Silk Shops were all searched, except for coarse cloth and Zhongshan cloth. The Nanhua shops used hemp bags to pack goods. Shuwange Silver Shop had already suffered huge losses last year, and this time it was searched by bandits several times, with no details spared. Dimao Rice Shop was robbed of dozens of stones of white rice. Since hearing the gunshots, the staff of Hengda Estate had all fled and hid. The manager and clerk, Mr. Xu and another person, feigned sleep in the dirty bedding of the old quartermaster and were not seen by the bandits. The iron box of the estate was strong, and the bandits used all their strength to knock on it. After two hours, they used all their strength to break the door and robbed 2,000 yuan in cash. They went upstairs to rummage through the boxes and cabinets. Seeing that there were no important items, they discarded them. Those residents who were robbed, such as Zhu Zhonghuang and the Yao family and more than ten households, only took cash, foreign currency, jewelry, and valuable leather clothes, but did not rob them. As for the earliest kidnapped person, Li Xinglin of Xiehe Pawnshop hid on the roof and was seen by the bandits with a flashlight and dragged down and taken away. In addition, those who were kidnapped were Fan Qirui of Yuanchang Clothing Store, Gu Jiesheng, Wang Jingbo, Sun Shuguan of Yitai Pawnshop, Mrs. Pan of Futairen, Shen Jingying, Shen Jingfang, Shen Wu Qingyan, Dai Lianfu of Jinlong, Zhu Xiangsheng, Dai Yunsheng, Wang Yulong's housewife, and girls, six of Zhu's family of seven, including Miss Senior, Miss Second, Miss Hua, Miss Asia, and Longguan, Wu Guihe of Hengfengchang, the housewife of Chen Yimao and her nine-year-old son, Jiang Weibin of Dingchang, and Huang Chenchu, the principal of the Liuxi School, and teacher Ling Jianming, etc. were taken to the Guandi Temple and separated. Well-known people such as Li Xinglin (who also serves as the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce) were slapped in the face because they did not tell their real names. The rest were judged by their clothes. It was heard that a certain storyteller and his wife were dressed gorgeously, and his wife was wearing a gold bracelet, which was almost mistaken for a wealthy family. After repeated explanations, their belongings were robbed and they were released. After the bandits finished questioning one by one, they said to the released people that they were quite disappointed that they had not been able to get to the god of wealth this time, and urged them to inform the family members of the hostages to raise money to redeem them, and there were many intimidating words. The Shanghai-Zhangyan ship was released because it had reached an agreement with the bandit leader Zhang Zhaohua. When the bandit leader was collecting the spoils in the Guandi Temple, the gang rules were strict, and it seemed that they were quite trained. However, the central banknotes were torn up. When the ship was about to leave, the bandit leader gave one dan of white rice, Shaoxing wine, ham, and other items, and then started the engine and returned. Seeing the bandit ship sailing towards Dianshan Lake, those with a little wealth in Zhangyan and nearby areas are now like frightened birds, and some have come to Songjiang to find a house to take refuge. Since Songjiang heard that Zhangyan was robbed by lake bandits, rumors spread for a while, and people were panicked, especially in the townships. The Jin County Governor immediately telegraphed the Songhu Garrison Command, requesting to send a team to Songjiang to increase defense. The 26th Regiment of the 13th Brigade of the 5th Division was sent to Songjiang on the 4th, and most of them were stationed at the headquarters. It is heard that tomorrow the companies will be assigned to Jinshan and Qingpu to suppress bandits and calm the area. Local communication.

Suzhou 76

The Municipal Government Reduces its Scope: The Suzhou Municipal Government, after being discussed and decided by the Provincial Government in principle to abolish and reduce its scope, has been handed over to the Department of Civil Affairs for review. It is now learned that the Department of Civil Affairs has decided to change it to a Municipal Bureau, and a clear order will arrive in Suzhou today.

President Lin of the Higher Court Requests an Increase in Prisoner Rations: President Lin of the Higher Court said that the price of rice has soared recently, and the original prisoner rations were set at 11 cents per prisoner per day, which is not enough to cover the costs. The wardens and prison officials of the counties have telegraphed to request an increase. After receiving the report, President Lin went to the province on the 3rd to attend yesterday's provincial government meeting, prepared a plan to increase the prisoner rations to maintain prison administration and avoid panic.

The Rampant Banditry in Various Townships in the County: According to bandit police reports, after the Yangsantaimiao Temple was burned down, the lake bandits fled to Weiting Fengli Village and Town. There are about 30 bandit ships, and the situation is very rampant. The district chief telegraphed to the province. More than ten bandit ships have also arrived at the Xinkai Road in Hengjing and are heading towards Wujiang. Fifteen bandit ships arrived in Chenmu Township yesterday (the 4th) morning and have been telegraphed to the County Bureau one after another. In addition to sending three platoons of police to Weiting to block them, Director Cao also reported to the Bandit Suppression Command and sent teams to Chenmu Xinkai Road and other places to search and suppress them. Also, Jin Guoshu, the acting magistrate of Changshu County, yesterday urgently reported that Yangsantaimiao Temple on the shore of Yangcheng Lake on the border of Suzhou and Changshu was burned down by the police team. Since then, the large gang of lake bandits has fled to the surface of Yangcheng Lake. He requested that a team be sent to assist in the suppression. After receiving the telegram, District Chief Gong immediately led a team of ships to search and suppress the area and requested the Bandit Suppression Command to send a team to assist in the suppression.

Request to Send Aircraft to Assist in Bandit Suppression: The Central Government previously ordered aircraft to be sent to Suzhou to assist the military and police in suppressing lake bandits. The banditry has only been slightly suppressed. Now, the Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression, Hu Zuyu, specially reported to the Commander-in-Chief's Office, requesting that two aircraft be sent to Suzhou to assist in the search and suppression. The Central Government has ordered Zhang Huichang, the Director of the Aviation Administration, to send aircraft to Suzhou to await dispatch as soon as the plan is drafted. In addition, Hu Zuyu, the Commander of the Bandit Suppression of Taihu Lake, sent official letters to various agencies yesterday, soliciting plans for bandit suppression.

Fengxian 77

Abolition of Local Security on a Regular Basis: The District Chief's Association previously stated that the local security system was cumbersome and proposed to abolish it immediately. The County Council re-deliberated and approved the proposal to set up a town and village police officer for each map to take over all previous local grain and security duties. The implementation is still under the county government and supervised by the town and village offices. It has been decided to order compliance from April 20.

The Wu Family's Accounting Ship Was Robbed: The accounting ship of the late wealthy Wu family in Shenhang was anchored in front of the house by the river. Yesterday night (2nd), more than a dozen bandits suddenly arrived, first tied up the shipworkers and prohibited them from making a sound, and then sailed towards Ruanxian Port. Later, neighbors heard about it and rushed to rescue them. A letter was found next to the shipworkers, signed by the Red Army, stating that the army needed ships and came to borrow them, and would return them within a month. It was also heard that there was a rifle and dozens of bullets on the ship, which were prepared for night defense. Now that there may be unforeseen circumstances in the future, the accounting house reported to the county today.

The County Issued a County-Wide Martial Law Order: The county police agencies, due to rumors of the robbery in neighboring Zhangyan, specially ordered the county to implement special martial law throughout the county from today (3rd) and ordered Team Captain Ding Zhiyan to go to block the area to avoid the bandits from fleeing.

Kunshan 78

County Magistrate Pang Has Taken Office: The new County Magistrate of Kunshan, Pang Shusen, arrived in Kunshan by car from Suzhou at 5:00 PM on the afternoon of the 3rd and went to the county government to meet the Acting County Magistrate Wang. Today (4th) at 10:00 AM, he first took over the office and then scheduled an oath.

The Impact of the Fire Brigade Not Being Resolved: The fire brigades in Kunshan's districts, because of a conflict with the members of the Public Security Bureau during a previous fire, were ordered by the former County Magistrate Wu to be arrested. As a result, the fire brigades were unwilling to put out the fires in the area. Previously, various agencies such as the District Office and the County Party Headquarters had sent letters inviting the executive members of the Fire Brigade Association and representatives of the main members of the fire brigades in each district to hold a joint meeting, but it was still unresolved. At 6:00 AM on the morning of the 4th, a fire broke out at the Beixin Chang Winery Warehouse outside the Daxi Gate, causing a fire. At that time, police sirens and gongs sounded, but the fire brigades still refused to put out the fire. Fortunately, there were many people in the winery, and the fire was quickly extinguished.

Wujiang 79

Conscripting Labor to Build Roads: It is heard that the county is conscripting labor to build roads. The original road lines were four roads. Now, Director Sun of the Construction Department believes that there are too many roads in the county, and it is difficult to conscript labor. He ordered the county to build the Fuhe Road to facilitate transportation. All miscellaneous tasks such as the Yingzhen laborers and substitutes along the Miaojing Road and other three roads must be transferred to the construction of the Fuhe Road.

Wuxi 80

A large number of refugees arrived at Meiyuan: About three to four hundred male and female refugees from Jiangbei Funing and other places suddenly arrived at Meiyuan, a famous scenic spot in this county located in Kaiyuan Township, which is usually crowded with tourists every spring and autumn. The refugees seemed intent on causing trouble. The security guard at the park gate reported this to the Ninth Branch of the Public Security Bureau, which dispatched police to suppress the situation, providing some travel expenses and escorting them out of the area.

Meeting on food relief for the people: Sun Zuji, the magistrate of this county, recognizing the recent soaring rice prices and the public's precarious food situation, specially convened a meeting yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM at the county government to discuss relief measures, inviting representatives from various government agencies, national bodies, and local gentry and wealthy individuals. The meeting focused on discussing ways to stabilize rice prices, suppress hoarding, and other solutions. Key resolutions were reached as follows: (1) Deciding on measures to implement price stabilization. It was resolved that the county government would supervise the district chiefs to actively solicit donations from the gentry and wealthy, with a deadline to collect the funds by the end of this month and report to the county government, after which price stabilization measures would be implemented regularly. Regarding the survey of civilian households, each district would supervise the township heads to conduct on-site investigations and verify registrations. (2) Planning to pre-order foreign rice futures to avoid procurement issues during emergencies. It was resolved that the Yicang Management Committee would immediately allocate 10,000 taels of silver from the accumulated losses to cooperate with local industry groups to purchase 1,000 tons of foreign rice for reserve. (3) Strictly prohibiting hoarding and speculation, and private export. It was resolved to investigate if people are hoarding, speculating, or privately exporting, and to allow people to report such actions at any time. A request was made to waive the feast tax. A dispute over the collection of the feast tax between the Wuxi County Education Bureau and the First District Office was recently resolved when the First District voluntarily conceded the tax collection to the Education Bureau. The Finance Department has ordered the county to submit the original case for review. However, Rongguan businesses, considering this case to be closely related to their industry, had previously submitted separate petitions to the National Government, the Executive Yuan, and the Jiangsu Provincial Government, requesting tax exemption. As no response had been received, the matter was brought up at the current County Chamber of Commerce Member Representative Assembly. It was argued that the fish, meat, seafood, sauces, wine, and oil used by these businesses are already subject to various taxes, and making Rong dishes, which are only for satisfying hunger, subject to another tax would be excessive. It was requested to grant an exemption from the feast tax, similar to the exemption granted by the Shanghai Special Municipality. The assembly unanimously passed the resolution, and the County Chamber of Commerce has recorded it and sent telegrams to the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the three departments of Finance, Civil Affairs, and Construction, requesting that the county be ordered to exempt the businesses from the tax to alleviate their difficulties.

Changzhou 81

Chairman Chiang passed through Changzhou: After inspecting troops in Shanghai, Chairman Chiang's train arrived at Changzhou Station at around 5:00 PM on the 3rd. A downward-bound express train simultaneously arrived at Changzhou Station, intersecting with Chiang's train. Coincidentally, former Chief of Civil Affairs, Miao Bin, was returning to Wuxi from Nanjing by train. Upon learning of Chairman Chiang's arrival in Changzhou, he boarded Chiang's train to pay his respects. They then disembarked together. Chairman Chiang went to the west end of the platform, turned back, and re-boarded the train. Miao respectfully saw him off at the station. The train stopped for about twenty minutes, and at 5:20 PM, the special train departed towards the capital. Resolutions of the County Administration Council: The Wu County Government convened a county administration meeting on the 3rd and resolved: (1) Rice prices have soared, reaching 17 yuan per picul. It was resolved to convene an emergency meeting on the 4th to maintain food supplies for the people. (2) The Second Sub-station of the Fourth Public Security Bureau detained three boats carrying rice for export in Weicun. It was resolved to send the rice boats to the county for instructions on how to handle them. (3) Dredging the canal, with orders to collect a surcharge of 30% on land tax. It was resolved to collect a surcharge of 10% during the slack season and 20% during the busy season and report to the Finance Department for record-keeping.

Nantong 82

Capture of the bandit leader in Eastern Township: The banditry in Nantong Eastern Township was rampant. After joint suppression by the navy, army, police, the bandits retreated to Caopeng Town. On the night of the 2nd, the Si Jiaba security team received a secret report and captured the bandit leader Jiang Laowu at Beishan Port. Upon learning of this, the county government dispatched six police squads in cars to escort Jiang Laowu on the morning of the 3rd. Dismissal of the Chief of the Urban Public Security Bureau: The Chief of the Urban Public Security Bureau, Long, was dismissed for gambling and feasting with two young women surnamed Yang and Zhou at Wolf Mountain at the end of last month, after being reported. On the 3rd, the County Public Security Bureau dismissed Long and handed him over to the county government for prosecution. The position of Chief of the Urban Public Security Bureau is temporarily held by Ling Changshou. The two women have suddenly disappeared, and their families are planning to file charges.

Construction of Dikes to Protect against Erosion in Yao and Wang Ports: The riverbanks of the Yao and Wang Ports are severely eroding. The Construction Bureau is implementing minor construction projects and building large dikes to take advantage of the high tide, while urgently repairing collapsed stonework. Issue of Lawyer Appearances in County Court: The Nantong County Court has temporarily suspended lawyer appearances because the Shanghai Bar Association has not yet sent notifications to the court. The local bar association has sent letters to the Shanghai association and reported the matter to the High Court for instructions.

Zhenjiang 83

Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department Pays Attention to Bandits: Hu, the Director of the Provincial Department of Civil Affairs, stated that banditry has been rampant in the province in recent years, with frequent kidnappings. The police have been exhausted trying to apprehend them. Recently, they have formed large gangs and are causing trouble everywhere along the lakeside and coastal areas, harming the good people. In order to plan for the eradication of banditry, a

Page 12

"Survey Form for Waterborne Bandits in This Province" was specifically designed and sent to each district, requiring them to report on both organized gangs and scattered groups in order to facilitate investigation and handling. Suining Party Headquarters Requests Police to Suppress Bandits: The executive committee of the Suining County Party Headquarters, due to the discovery of large numbers of bandits in the county looting, killing, and burning, causing great distress to the people, resolved to send representatives to the province to visit Zhang Yuanyang, a standing committee member of the Provincial Party Headquarters, to request that the Provincial Government be consulted and ordered the Civil Affairs Department to send provincial police to suppress the bandits. It is reported that after receiving the request, the Provincial Department has already consulted the Provincial Government and ordered the Civil Affairs Department to send police to suppress the bandits and pacify the area. Petition to Abolish River Management Expenses: Shipowners from various counties previously protested the Construction Department's collection of river management expenses, which were deducted from ship tickets. They sent representatives to petition the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Transportation for the abolition of the fees. The Ministry of Transportation approved an investigation and ordered a review, but the matter has been pending for half a year without resolution. With the arrival of the new Provincial Committee, representatives from various counties plan to re-petition to fundamentally resolve the issue. They then went to the Construction Department to petition, where Director Sun personally met with them. The representatives stated that the surcharge was difficult to handle. Yangzhou 84

Provincial Committee Member Wang Visits Yangzhou: Wang Bailing, a provincial committee member of the Provincial Government, came to Yangzhou to attend the shareholders meeting of the Zhenyang Automobile Company, which was previously adjourned, and rescheduled for 3:00 PM on the 3rd. Merchants Request Invitation to Take Over Operations: Deshe Tai, He Cheng, and Quanji, food merchants, previously reported that the market was flooded with smuggled salt, causing official sales to stagnate and losses to their capital. They requested the recruitment of new merchants. Their request was approved and they were encouraged to continue operating with difficulty. As they were unable to sustain themselves, they submitted a subsequent report. Yesterday (the 2nd), Zhang, the transport commissioner, not only approved the report but also ordered the Anti-Smuggling Bureau to carry out reforms to increase official sales and relieve the merchants' difficulties. Search for Robbers in Pagoda Bay Ferry Robbery Case: In the previous Pagoda Bay ferry robbery case in this county, the Sixth District of Water Police in Gaoyou learned that Wang's family, residing in the Bingmasi Alley inside the Xiaodongmen of Yangzhou City, was a major suspect. The district chief immediately dispatched more than ten police officers to Yangzhou by boat. Yesterday (the 2nd) at 5:00 PM, they went to investigate and apprehend Wang. Wang himself had already fled upon hearing the news. Two short barrel pistols were found during the search of his home. Wang's wife was taken back to the inn for detailed questioning. It was also reported that the water police had taken Wang's wife back to Gaoyou this morning for interrogation. At 5:00 PM this afternoon, the Datong Ferry Company's small ferry traveling from Zhenjiang to Gaoyou passed through Sanmao Temple in this county, and the district police dispatched a team to search the ship again. It was heard that one bandit was found.

Jingjiang 85

Ningjie Market Robbed Again: Ningjie Market, located in the northern part of this county and bordering Tai and Ru, was previously visited by bandits once. Unexpectedly, on the night of the 31st of last month, several bandits with weapons swarmed in, first entering Chen Xien's home to loot extensively, then robbing three or four more homes before leaving with shouts. Second District Security Sub-group Burned Down by Bandits: The Ninth Security Sub-group of the Second District was located in Donglai Nunnery, a strategic location at the border between Ru and Jing. The district commander, concerned about its insufficient strength, transferred the soldiers of the Fourth Sub-group of Wuwugang and the Flower Lai Nunnery branch to that location. On the morning of March 30th at 3:00 AM, more than two hundred bandits secretly infiltrated the area from Changjiuwuqiao, ambushing the sub-group from all sides. Three scouts were sent to probe near the group headquarters. When the soldiers on patrol questioned them for the password, the scouts remained silent. The soldiers fired a warning shot, and the bandits returned fire with their Mauser pistols, hitting soldier Zhang Wenyi in the lower body. Hearing the sound, the soldiers inside prepared urgently. The ambushing bandits then surrounded them from all sides. The soldiers exited through the back door and fought bravely, but they were outnumbered and gradually overwhelmed. They temporarily retreated. The bandits then set fire to the two front rooms and one middle room of the group headquarters. By the time the provincial police and the district headquarters arrived, the bandits had fled.

Gaoyou 86

Bandits Rob Two Villages in One Night: On the night of the 31st, more than ten bandits suddenly arrived in Chen Village in this county, each armed with guns, searching and robbing house by house and shooting and wounding one farmer. It is estimated that clothing, silver, and foreign currency worth approximately 1,000 to 2,000 yuan were looted. On the same night, several small boats carrying dozens of bandits arrived at Hanliu Village, each armed with knives and guns, and swarmed ashore to rob farmers. After the village head reported to the district headquarters, District Chief Zhu led the militia to the village and engaged the bandits in a fierce battle for three hours. The bandits were finally defeated and fled south by boat. Subsequently, Officer Hu of the Public Security Sub-station led the police to track and pursue them, capturing one bandit boat and five bandits at Qiujia Mansion. They were escorted to the city last night and handed over to the county for prosecution.

Qingpu 87

Meeting of the County Party Affairs Reorganization Committee: The Qingpu County Party Affairs Reorganization Committee held its seventh committee meeting yesterday and resolved: (1) The Pharmaceutical Workers Union submitted a request to find ways to support unemployed members. The committee resolved to instruct the pharmaceutical district committee to prioritize hiring unemployed members. (2) The Xu Xiulie Martyr Monument has not yet been built and should be started immediately to comfort the spirit of the martyr and provide a memorial. The committee resolved to hand it over to the secretariat to draft a plan for further discussion. (3) Regarding the case of Zhang Hanchu and Gu Zhibin, whose party membership was revoked by a previous executive committee, the province has not yet issued a clear order for implementation. The committee resolved to request the province to promptly review and revoke their membership and hand it over to the training department for handling. (4) Regarding the case of Ke Jie and ten other citizens of the Eleventh District, who accused Tan Dingyi, a police officer of the First Sub-station of the Public Security Bureau in that district, of malfeasance, corruption, and dereliction of duty, after investigation, the facts have been verified. The committee resolved to send a letter to the county government ordering the Public Security Bureau to promptly dismiss the police officer. A Bizarre Case of a Lost Daughter-in-Law: Lu Youxiang, a farmer from Xiwaihe Village near Zhujiajiao Town in Qingpu County, has two sons, Hongqing and Yunqing. Last spring, Hongqing married Zhou Maolong's daughter Xiugu from Sanwan Village. After the marriage, the couple did not get along well. Unexpectedly, Xiugu suddenly ran away last month without a trace. After losing his daughter-in-law, Lu ordered his son Yunqing to go to Shanghai to find her. The next day, Lu also went to Shanghai to search, but there was no news. On the way, he met his eldest son, Hongqing, who said that his sister-in-law had been found and was working as a maid in a mansion and would be able to return home at the end of the month. They might as well return home first. Unexpectedly, when the time came, Lu asked his eldest son, Hongqing, for money and went to Shanghai again the day before yesterday to urge his sister-in-law to return home. Hongqing returned to his hometown yesterday with his sister-in-law Xiugu. For some reason, his uncle, Shen Yinglin, suddenly detained him, suspecting that he had abducted and absconded, and sent him to the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau for punishment.

Jiaxing 88

District Heads Have Been Appointed: The Jiaxing County Government, during the fourth meeting of village representatives convened by the county government to divide districts, decided to divide the county into seven districts. Yesterday, the district heads of each district were appointed by the Department of Civil Affairs: Shang Baoshan, Mo Shancheng, Mei Shouren, Zhu Jipan, Wang Ziliang, Liu Shupang, and Pan Qinghua were appointed. After being appointed, the district heads will be sworn in as soon as the office locations are confirmed. The Farmers Bank Preparatory Office is Issuing Loans: Since the establishment of the Jiaxing Farmers Bank Preparatory Office, the opening date has been pending because the fund has not yet been fully funded. Now, Director Wu has submitted a request to the province to approve an allocation of 10,000 yuan to test the issuance of loans, as the silkworm season is approaching and farmers need funds. The lightest interest rate is taken, and each rural cooperative guarantees borrowing from the Farmers Bank Preparatory Office and re-lending it to farmers for their needs. Now that this news has spread, applications for loans from rural cooperatives have been pouring in. Director Wu believes that the planned 10,000 yuan is not enough to distribute, so he has submitted a request to the county government to forward it to the province for approval to continue allocating 5,000 yuan to increase the number of loans.

Jiashan 89

Bandit Atmosphere is Rampant in the County: Robberies and kidnappings in Jiashan County occur every day. Last night, the home of Li A'er in Nangu Village, Dingpeng District, was invaded by bandits, who carried out a looting spree. All the rice money, more than 270 foreign dollars, was completely robbed, and 37 piculs of white rice were also robbed by the bandits. The owner of the incident was also wounded in the right arm with a knife. Also, the home of Jin Xiaodi in Jinjiabin held a Buddhist ceremony last night and bandits broke in, looting wildly. The monks were bound and prevented from moving. Then they rummaged through boxes and chests, looting everything. The total loss of clothing was more than 500 yuan.

Yongfu West Village Closed Down: In the ferry robbery case on Qianjing Pond the other day, Wang Angru, the partner of Yongfu Village in Xitang, had 5,000 yuan looted. The village decided to close down due to the dangerous navigation routes and merge with Jiashan. All households have been notified separately. Xitang's False Alarm for Three Days: District Chief Su Gongguoliang telegraphed District Chief Zhao, reporting that a large group of lake bandits had robbed Zhangyan and threatened to rob Xitang, requesting attention and ordering to block and defend. Su dispatched teams to pursue and suppress. District Chief Zhao immediately telegraphed Chen Boang, the eighth captain of Xitang, to pay close attention. On one hand he dispatched teams to rush West overnight to meet them. On the other hand, Xitang received the news and immediately closed the market. Many timid people fled to the city. Police and militia patrolled with live ammunition and the local situation was very tight.

Exchange of Vouchers: Since Chairman Zhuang approved the prior issuance of 500,000 yuan of Zhejiang Relief Public Bond exchange vouchers, preparations have been actively made. Zhejiang Province Sets a Date for County Magistrate Examinations: In addition to Zhu Jiahua, Chen Bulei, and Ma Yinchu, who are outside the province, the county magistrate examination committee members, including Guo Xincong, Rao Yan, Huang Xuyuan, and Zhang Naiyan, all arrived in Hangzhou on the evening of the 2nd and held the first examination committee meeting at the Civil Affairs Department at 9:00 AM on the 3rd. Chuzhou 91

The Piteous State of Chuzhou: Xu Nan, the magistrate of Chuxian County, Hou Bo, the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, and He Zhixuan, the director of the local financial management office, reported that the disasters in Chuzhou, including war, bandits, drought, and locusts, have been particularly severe and urgently require assistance. Now, as the period between crops is approaching, the disasters in each district are intensifying. The piteous cries of the people are everywhere, and those seeking death in their families are not uncommon. Even those fortunate enough to wait for death can only eat elm bark once a day. Recently, a large number of refugees gathered and surrounded the county government, ready to riot. There are currently more than 30,000 people in urgent need of relief to survive, and about 10,000 households without seeds for autumn crops. The current situation is unsustainable, and a major disaster is imminent. A telegram was sent on behalf of all the people to the Chinese Health Society, the Chinese Red Cross Society, the Huayang Charity Relief Association, and other charitable organizations, requesting generous emergency relief to save the affected people. It is hoped that kind-hearted gentlemen, upon seeing this tragic situation, will not hesitate to contribute generously.

Local News

Commander Xiong Sends Troops to Suppress Lake Bandits 92

▲Orders All Counties to Encircle and Suppress Regardless of Jurisdiction

The Songhu Garrison Command, in response to the looting by lake bandits in Zhangyan Town and Hejingwan and other places in Jinshan County, has ordered the Second Company of the Artillery Battalion of the Fifth Division stationed in Longhua to be stationed in Songjiang to pursue and suppress the bandits. Yesterday, the Command also ordered the Third Battalion of the Twenty-sixth Regiment of the Thirteenth Brigade of the Fifth Division stationed in Longhua, led by Battalion Commander Zeng Yisheng, with the Ninth, Tenth, Eleventh, and Third Companies, to depart from Longhua at 10:40 AM yesterday, traveling in eight passenger cars attached to the 22nd freight train from Shanghai to Hangzhou to Songjiang, separately to pursue and suppress the bandits. The Songhu Garrison Command yesterday issued an order to the military, police, and various government agencies under its jurisdiction: "Investigation reveals that lake bandits have been accumulating in Taihu Lake. The Taihu Bandit Suppression Headquarters has divided the counties along the lake, including Wuxi, Wuxian, Wujin, Changxing, Yixing, and Wujiang, into bandit suppression zones to carry out suppression. In order to fundamentally eliminate bandits, if lake bandits infiltrate this garrison area in the future, they should be temporarily encircled and suppressed in cooperation with local military and police, regardless of jurisdiction. The county magistrates should also closely monitor bandit activity and report it to this Command and directly to the Taihu Bandit Suppression Headquarters to facilitate prevention and suppression. In addition to separate orders, you are hereby urgently ordered to comply with and instruct all subordinates to comply."

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau Strives to Stabilize Rice Prices 93

▲30,000 Picul of Rice Stored in Heshang

▲Must Fall by Two Yuan Within Ten Days

▲Order to Report Rice Hoarding According to Regulations

▲Rice Prices in Rice Shops Must Be Made Public

According to Wuchen News Agency, rice supplies have gradually increased in recent days, and prices in the interior have also stabilized. There is a gradual hope of rice prices falling. Yesterday, the highest grade of white rice opened at 19.5 yuan, but due to the unsatisfied desires of a few rice merchants who colluded with each other, prices have remained high. The Social Affairs Bureau is paying close attention to the situation. Yesterday, in addition to continuing to send personnel to the north and south markets to investigate and advise, it strictly ordered the rice industry associations to comply with the previous order to reduce rice prices by two yuan within ten days and not to obstruct it secretly. Details are as follows:

▲More than 20,000 Picul of Rice Stored in the North Market: The Bureau sent personnel to meet with Jiang Shizhi, the Standing Committee Member of the Shanghai North Rice Grain Marketing Association, and found that more than 200 rice boats were docked in Heshang, carrying tens of thousands of picul of rice. The current price of Changshu's top-grade rice is 19.5 yuan, which is 50 cents less than yesterday. The market is continuing to decline, so the general marketers and boatmen are still holding high prices and refusing to sell. They should sell all the rice according to the market price immediately. If they continue to wait, it will be enforced. The same warning was also given to the Changshu Rice Merchants Association.

▲Sixty Rice Boats in the South Market: A total of 31 rice boats arrived in the past two days, and the total number of rice boats accumulated in the past few days has reached 64, carrying 8,002 picul of rice. Most of them are self-selling boats, totaling 19 boats carrying 2,655 picul of rice. Chen Qinji and Zhang Chengji each have 8 boats with more than 1,900 picul of rice. Yan Xiaoji has 9 boats with 1,210 picul of rice. In addition, marketers each have several hundred picul. As of last night, none of the above rice had been sold. The Social Affairs Bureau selected those who insisted on not selling and warned them. If they still do not sell, there will be appropriate measures to execute.

▲Strict Order to Warn Rice Merchants: The Social Affairs Bureau has learned of various tricks from merchants, so it has ordered various rice industry groups to state that the Bureau previously stipulated that the highest white rice price would be temporarily limited to 20 yuan and ordered it to be reduced by two yuan within ten days. It has been found that the number of rice boats in Heshang has not decreased recently, and the rice that has not been sold is more than 10,000 picul every day. The market in the producing area has also declined, and the rice price should have fallen, but it is still high. It is clear that someone is manipulating it. After investigation, it was found that some rice merchants have greed and colluded with rice merchants in the producing areas to deliberately hold back sales and prevent rice from being shipped to Shanghai and sent important personnel to Wuxi and other places to negotiate a large-scale manipulation plan. It has also been heard that Hakka rice dealers have also telegraphed overseas producing areas to temporarily stop shipping to see what the market will do. Furthermore, unscrupulous merchants are falsely claiming to be transporting grain and exporting it. Although the above information is based on rumors, it is not without reason based on the local rice market situation. The Bureau is concerned day and night about maintaining the food supply for 2.7 million people, but a few rice merchants are disregarding the overall situation and arbitrarily disrupting it. The Bureau hereby reorders the association to inform the industry not to repeat the old practices, to only seek private interests, to disregard the people's livelihood, and to harm public order. It is still important to strictly abide by the previous order and reduce the price of each picul of rice by two yuan within ten days and be responsible for clearing the source of the producing area and not secretly obstructing it. If there is still a refusal to sell, the Bureau will only take the interests of the majority as its own interests and execute appropriate measures. This is not a forewarning. The order is urgent.

▲Order to Report Rice Hoarding: The Social Affairs Bureau has repeatedly sent personnel to find that various rice companies have a large amount of rice stored but do not report it. There are also times when rice is stored in the interior but not shipped to Shanghai. Therefore, it has issued a notice to various rice industry groups, stating that the regulations for the public hoarding of rice require that the hoarding of rice be registered with the Bureau. All hoarding merchants should strictly comply with it to avoid accusations and to maintain the people's food supply. However, it has been found that various rice merchants have delayed in complying and there are still private hoarding situations. The associations must inform their industry to report all the rice stored in each warehouse by the 8th of this month. The rice stored in this warehouse should also be reported every day for the Bureau's investigators to take to the Bureau for verification. If there is any concealment, once it is found, it will be reported to the mayor and severely punished for hoarding and disrupting the people's food supply.

▲Order to Publicly Set Rice Prices: The sale of rice by rice shops is directly related to consumers. Recently, the rice market has been chaotic and a few rice merchants have taken the opportunity to profit. Therefore, it is ordered that the Jiagu Public Office state that the Public Office has previously negotiated and announced rice prices on a daily basis, and all the industry followed the prices for sale to avoid market chaos. The law is very good and should be restored in the current situation of high rice prices to stabilize market prices and benefit the people's livelihood. The Public Office is ordered to comply with this order and from the date of receipt of the order, it will publicly discuss the prices of first, second, and third grade japonica and indica rice every day and notify all members of the industry to comply, and publish it in the newspaper and report the compliance. The order is urgent.

Sino-Japanese Legal Rights Negotiations 94

▲Foreign Minister Wang Personally Delivers Draft

▲Envoy Shigemitsu Awaits Instructions for Talks

The Sino-Japanese negotiations regarding legal rights are about to formally begin. According to sources in diplomatic circles, during Foreign Minister Wang's recent visit to Shanghai, he met with Acting Envoy Shigemitsu. Foreign Minister Wang personally presented the four articles of the draft for China's abolition of consular jurisdiction (specifically for Japan) drafted by the National Government to Minister Aoi Shigemitsu. Shigemitsu expressed his acceptance and has already telegraphed them to the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs for review. Once instructions are received in Shanghai, formal negotiations can begin. Foreign Minister Wang will also meet with Mr. Shigemitsu in Shanghai this Saturday to discuss the case orally.

Release of Yangtze River Steamers Arrives in Shanghai 98

Six Ships Arrive Simultaneously. In order to maintain Yangtze River traffic, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, through the efforts of Business Section Chief Li Yunliang in Hankou, has arranged for three major Yangtze River steamers to return to Shanghai to provide shipping services. With the agreement of Shipping Department Chief Qiu Wei, the Jiangxin, Jianghua, and Jiangshun steamers were released on the same day. Yesterday afternoon, these three steamers arrived in Shanghai from Hankou. The Jiangyu steamer, released by the Communications Department, also arrived at the same time. The Sanbei Company's Xin Ningxing steamer also sent a telegram yesterday stating that it had departed from Hankou and was expected to arrive today. The Yongxing steamer of the Ning Shao Company also went downriver to Shanghai last night. It is found that six Chinese steamers arrived in the Yangtze River in one day, and all can be ordered to operate, but the goods loaded on each ship are very scarce.

Order to Collect Rental Fees. Yesterday, various shipping companies in Shanghai received a telegram from the Communications Department of the Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force stating that the unpaid rent, coal, and river fees owed to the shipping companies last year have now been fully received. The payment is scheduled to be made in full on the 7th of this month. However, since the previous receipts issued by the companies were temporary civilian receipts and did not comply with the reimbursement regulations, a standardized invoice has now been prescribed. It is necessary to extract the amount of payments received by each company in May, August, September, October, and November of last year, fill them in, and bring them to Nanjing along with the charter agreements and seals in order to clear all the ship rental payments. Yesterday, various companies were rushing to prepare detailed invoices for the collection of fees and were preparing to send representatives to Nanjing within the next two days to collect the funds.

Siamese King's Nephew Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday 99

The Da Wan Bao newspaper reports that Prince Yugala, the nephew of the King of Siam, has been studying in Europe and America for ten years. He has now been summoned back to his country by the King and arrived in Shanghai on the President Grant from San Francisco today. He will disembark for a short visit and then continue south on the same ship. Currently, the King of Siam still has nephews, and only one of his brothers also has a son. Therefore, the Prince has a good chance of inheriting the throne in the future.

Geshe Lama Can Arrive Today 100

▲Will Enter Tibet to Persuade the Living Buddha to Lean Inward

Lama Geshe Dorje Jigme, who was invited by the Buddhist Association of Chengdu, Sichuan to give lectures, and who brought a large number of Buddhist images and scriptures with him, has traveled south from Beiping by sea and is expected to arrive in Shanghai today. The Shanghai Buddhist Association has publicly nominated him to promote Buddhism and will welcome him upon his arrival in Shanghai. He will stay in Shanghai for about three or four days before transferring to a Yangtze River ship to enter Sichuan. The primary reason the authorities in Sichuan have invited Geshe Lama to the province is to ask him to persuade the Living Buddha of Tibet to lean inward and accept the rule of the National Government, and not to be misled by the Mongolian Youth Party. Therefore, when Geshe Lama traveled south through Pingjin, the Sichuan Provincial Government specifically telegraphed instructions to all locations along the route to provide him with special treatment, free transportation by land and water, and escorts along the way, to show their respect.

Municipal Government Compiles Budget for the 19th Year 108

▲Organizing the Budget Committee to Begin Discussion

▲Efforts Will Be Made to Economize on Both Regular and Temporary Expenses

The Xin Shanghai News Agency reports that the Shanghai Special Municipality Municipal Government has been established for nearly three years. In the past 16th year, the total actual revenue was more than 3.54 million yuan, and the actual expenditure was more than 3.36 million yuan. Although there was a surplus on the books, more than 600,000 yuan was owed in temporary expenses. The revenue budget for the 17th year was more than 3.37 million yuan, of which more than 600,000 yuan was directly spent by the municipal treasury, and the rest was used to cover the regular needs of each bureau. Various temporary expenses were not included. Fortunately, after taking over the urban area, revenue increased sharply. The actual revenue was more than 4.275 million yuan, and the actual expenditure also reached more than 4.396 million yuan. The balance of revenue and expenditure showed a shortfall of more than 112,000 yuan. Together with the unpaid expenses of various departments, there was a total shortfall of more than 600,000 yuan. The revenue budget for the 18th year was more than 5.05 million yuan, and the expenditure was more than 5.06 million yuan. Temporary expenses were not included. It is heard that when compiling the previous budget, it was originally intended to allocate a reserve fund to cover temporary needs. However, due to the development of the business of each department, it was insufficient to allocate, so the old figures were used as regular expenses, and temporary revenue was used to supplement temporary expenses. However, on the expenditure side, since the budget was announced, additional expenses have been added one after another due to business development, totaling more than 190,000 yuan. As the year has not yet ended, it is difficult to investigate the financial situation of the whole year. However, it is heard that the total report for this year shows a shortfall of more than 160,000 yuan. It is difficult to clear all regular expenses, but there is a huge amount of more than 180,000 yuan in unpaid temporary expenses. As for the situation in the second half of the year, on the revenue side, no new taxes have been added. Under the land tax item, the North Expedition donation has been canceled, resulting in a reduction of more than 80,000 yuan. The accumulated housing rent has been collected, and there is no increase in revenue. The only item that has the hope of increasing revenue is the ship tax. On the expenditure side, regular expenses have continued to increase, and the temporary expenses that have been approved total about 200,000 yuan. By the end of the year, they will also be considerable. Therefore, it can be predicted that the financial situation in the second half of the year will be tighter than in the first half of the year. Now, with the beginning of the 19th year approaching, the Municipal Government has organized a budget committee to start discussion on April 1. The budget for the 19th year will be carefully considered to correct the mistakes of the past. Efforts will be made to economize on regular expenses, and special attention will be paid to temporary expenses. The Finance Bureau, due to the establishment and implementation of the budget, is responsible for the lifeline of the city's operations and has appointed Xu Dun, the chief of the Third Section, to preside over everything.

Jianghai Customs Burns Opium Yesterday 110

▲Valued at More Than 120,000 Yuan

Jianghai Customs burned opium at the Lu Jiazui Steam Kiln in Pudong yesterday. Commissioner Pan Fubian, who was entrusted by the Supervisory Office, went to the Customs at 8:00 AM to meet with Customs Representative Ge Yixin, Warehouse Manager Robert, and more than a dozen Chinese and Western guards. The prohibited items were transported from the Customs warehouse to a small steamer along with coolies. Inspectors from various agencies, including Ye Liangguang from the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, Yao Yanyun from the Shanghai Local Court, Ji Shiying and Zhou Chucai from the Anti-Opium Association of the Republic of China, gathered at the Customs Wharf and crossed the Huangpu River on a small steamer. Director Yuan of the Municipal Public Security Bureau specifically appointed Zhang Mingqin, the district chief of the Third District, to lead a platoon of armed police officers to take care of the scene. Then, Robert ordered the cook to light the coal in one or two kilns at the same time, and the opium was weighed and verified by everyone. The burning began at 9:00 AM and ended at 10:45 AM. A total of 30 dan, 82 jin, and 10 liang of Yunshi and Chuanshi opium were burned, with an estimated value of more than 124,520 silver yuan. In addition, more than 1 dan and 43 jin and 8 liang of counterfeit opium sent by a certain agency was also thrown into the kiln for burning. Furthermore, items such as morphine-containing medicinal water and medicine were valued at 324.58 silver yuan, and numerous nude female photos were also burned in the kiln. Two wooden boxes of opium lamp covers and opium pipes, valued at 246.50 silver yuan, were ordered by the coolies to be dumped on the ground and smashed with hammers. Afterwards, Commissioner Pan accompanied the inspectors to the Customs School for a short rest, tea, and snacks before dispersing.

County Government Sends Personnel to Investigate Opium Seedlings 111

The Shanghai County Government has received an instruction from the National Anti-Opium Association forwarded by the Civil Affairs Department, stating that it is now springtime, which is the time when poppies emerge. It is necessary to urgently order the county magistrate to conduct a thorough investigation in accordance with the inspection methods and report the results within one month after receiving the document. News on the Agreement Between the Municipal Government and the Gas Company 116

Conditions Agreed Upon: Signing Imminent

The Municipal Government, considering the British Shanghai Gas Company's business operations within the Chinese territory, urged the company to enter into an agreement to define its rights and obligations. The Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities was responsible for handling the matter, but negotiations had been ongoing for years without a satisfactory resolution. Recently, through several rounds of negotiations, both parties reached a general agreement on the conditions. On March 28th, the company, in accordance with Article 11 of the agreement, paid a deposit of $1,820 to the Bureau of Public Utilities, which was then transferred to the Bureau of Finance. On April 3rd, the company's Chief Engineer, Mr. Butt, visited the Bureau for discussions, and an agreement was reached on amending Article 8 regarding the Municipal Government's deadline for ordering the relocation of gas pipes. Yesterday (the 4th) at 2:00 PM, the Bureau held formal negotiations with the company again. Those present on the Municipal Government side included Mr. Huang, Director of the Bureau of Public Utilities, Mr. Shen, Director of the Bureau of Public Works, and Mr. Zhu, Section Chief of the Second Section of the Bureau of Public Utilities. On the company side were Mr. Canning, Chairman, and Mr. Butt, Chief Engineer. As a result, the company representatives fully acknowledged the terms of the agreement, and both parties agreed to complete the contract signing formalities next Monday, Tuesday, or Wednesday, and then formally sign the agreement. The gas agreement issue, which had been causing problems for over a year, is now said to be coming to a conclusion.

Local News Two

Detailed Report on the Robbery of the Shanghai-Zhangyan Steamer

▲ The Steamer Returned to Shanghai the Day Before Yesterday

▲ The Purser Was Kidnapped and Released

Zhangyan Town in Jinshan County, approximately 180 miles from Shanghai, was suddenly looted by bandits on Tuesday evening this week. They first robbed the town's Public Security Bureau and security corps of their firearms, and then proceeded to loot shops and residences. Larger pawnshops, jewelry stores, and foreign goods shops were all affected, resulting in incalculable losses. Furthermore, over fifty male and female students were kidnapped, and two members of the security corps were killed. The details have already been recorded in the important news section of this newspaper. However, after the bandits kidnapped people and property, the Shanghai-Zhangyan steamer "Shanghai-Zhang" of the Shanghai-Zhangyan Shipping Bureau on Beijing Road happened to be sailing from Shanghai to Zhangyan. When it docked at the riverbank, the bandits noticed it and boarded to loot it. They also ordered the crew to start the fire and towed over thirty bandit boats carrying the kidnapped male and female students and items such as gold, silver, and valuables, along with over three hundred bandits, to the Guanwang Temple, about eighty miles from the town. Zhang Zongling and Wang Qingming, the pursers of the Shanghai-Zhangyan steamer, were also kidnapped and held for a night until around 11:00 AM the next morning when the bandit leader ordered them to be released, allowing them to escape danger. At the same time, twenty or thirty of the kidnapped male and female students were also released and returned to the town on the steamer. The Shanghai-Zhangyan steamer returned to Shanghai the day before yesterday, recording the incident of encountering bandits, being robbed, and being forced to tow boats in this manner.

▲ The Shanghai-Zhangyan Steamer Encounters Bandits

The Shanghai-Zhangyan steamer set sail at 8:00 AM on Tuesday (i.e., April 1st), heading straight for Zhangyan Town. There were over a hundred passengers and some cargo on board. At around 4:00 PM, it arrived at Zhangyan and docked between Anmin Bridge and Lime Kiln. Passengers disembarked one after another, and the cargo was also unloaded at the same time. The crew was sweeping the deck, preparing to rest until around 5:30 PM when they were about to boil water for dinner. Suddenly, gunshots were heard in the air, coming closer from a distance. The crew could not help but be greatly alarmed. Members of the security corps on the shore stated that there were thirty or forty civilian boats coming in the water, which they suspected were bandits, and they had ordered a curfew, prohibiting passage on the river surface at night. Before long, the bandit boats had sailed straight in, mooring from Anmin Bridge to Lime Kiln, blocking the Shanghai-Zhangyan steamer at both ends. At this time, the purser's room had already learned of the robbery in the town and knew that they would not be spared if the bandits came. Therefore, the entire ship prepared for defense, planning a retreat.

▲ The Purser Disguises Himself as a Tea Boy

Zhang Zongling and Wang Qingming, the pursers of the steamer, were quick-witted in a crisis. They handed the keys to the accounts cabinet to the tea boy, removed their long gowns, disguised themselves as servants, and waited quietly for the bandits to arrive. A few minutes later, two bandits boarded the ship and entered the cabin. Seeing Zhang Zongling, they asked, "What kind of person are you? Are you the purser?" Zhang replied that the purser had already gone ashore and that he was a tea boy. The bandits looked at him several times and said nothing more. They then entered the purser's room and robbed over forty dollars in banknotes. After a while, three more bandits came to search before leaving the ship. Around 6:00 PM, a sudden influx of bandits, all speaking with a northern accent, acted rudely, wielding various weapons such as Mauser pistols. They forced the captain to start the fire and set sail. The crew, forced by the bandits' intimidation, had no choice but to obey.

▲ Towing Boats Like a Long Serpent

There were a total of thirty-four bandit boats, each carrying seven, eight, or more than ten bandits. The kidnapped male and female students and villagers were hidden under reed mats. Zhang Zongling, the purser of the Shanghai-Zhangyan steamer, was also kidnapped onto a small boat. Thus, the bandit boats were connected like a long serpent, being towed by the steamer. Because there were too many boats being towed, the progress was very slow along the way. The bandits became impatient and often spoke harshly to the captain and threatened him with guns. After being told that there were too many boats and too much weight, making it impossible to speed up, the bandits reluctantly fell silent. They set off from Zhangyan at around 6:00 PM on the 1st and arrived at the Guanwang Temple at around 6:00 AM the next morning. The journey from Zhangyan was only about eighty miles, but it took twelve hours, showing how slow the progress was.

▲ Dividing the Spoils at Guanwang Temple

The boats arrived at Guanwang Temple and stopped. The bandits escorted all the hostages ashore one by one, and carried boxes and baskets, removing all the stolen goods such as gold, silver, valuables, clothes, and utensils. They transported them to the open space in front of the Guanwang Temple and temporarily stored them there. The bandit leader set up an incense table, burned incense, and silently prayed before dividing the spoils on the spot. Various stolen goods were piled up separately, such as gold and silver jewelry in one pile and clothes in another pile. The kidnapped men and women were also divided into teams and the bandit leader carefully inquired about their family backgrounds and looked at their clothing to decide who to keep and who to release. Those kept were escorted back to the bandit boats, and those released were temporarily held in the open space. The bandits divided the spoils, taking the silver and getting the gold, silver utensils were thrown away and ignored, and gold utensils were cherished and stored carefully. The value of gold over silver has increased further. At noon, the purser of the Shanghai-Zhangyan steamer, who had been kidnapped, begged the bandits to release the boat so that it could resume business. The bandits initially refused but finally agreed after much pleading. So, they left Guanwang Temple at around 11:00 AM that morning and returned to the town. Before leaving, the bandits sent over thirty hostages back to the steamer to be taken back to Zhangyan. The crew of the Shanghai-Zhangyan steamer felt as if they had been reborn and celebrated with joy. The steamer sailed to the Chuanlai Temple area in Songjiang and met the Shen-Zhang steamer that was sailing from Shanghai to Zhangyan. They transferred the more than thirty hostages who were released to the other boat to return to Zhangyan, while the Shanghai-Zhangyan went straight to Shanghai and arrived safely. This morning, it resumed sailing to Zhangyan.

▲ Investigation of Business Losses

Pawnshop: Yilai - approximately 25,000 yuan, manager Gu Jiesheng and five employees kidnapped; Xiehe - over 6,000 yuan, manager Li Xinglin and employees Wang Jingbo and Zhu Zhonghuang kidnapped; Clothing Store: Yuyuan - over 10,000 yuan, also a silver box carried away; Yongzengxiang - over 8,000 yuan; Yuanchang - over 2,000 yuan, manager Fan Qirui kidnapped, already released yesterday; Money Exchange: Hengda - due to preparedness, only about 1,000 yuan; Silk and Satin: Hengtaixiang - over 5,000 yuan; Foreign Goods: Xiechangxiang - 2,000 yuan, Dashengxiang - 1,000 yuan, Lihua - 1,000 yuan, Futairen - 1,000 yuan, the wife of shop owner Pan Laosi kidnapped; Jewelry Store: Shuwanhe - over 5,000 yuan; Rice Shop: Dingmao - two boats of rice stolen, approximately 3,000 yuan, Fengtai - 4,000 yuan; Sauce Shop: Wanheng - 1,000 yuan, Gonghe - 1,000 yuan; Dried Goods: Xiesheng - over 1,000 yuan, Rongchang - 1,000 yuan; Pharmacy: Jiang Tianyou - 1,000 yuan, Jishengtang - 400 yuan, a son, a daughter-in-law, and two daughters kidnapped; Other: Pan Shun Gongxing Hotel - 1,000 yuan, Yongshengxiang Tea Shop - 400 yuan, Jiang Tianyou Pickles Shop - 1,000 yuan, the post office - an iron box carried away; four women from the Shen family kidnapped, three young daughters of Zhu Zhonghuang's family in the Lao Tianbao Jewelry Store kidnapped, losses of approximately 300 yuan. The losses of other families, ranging from a few hundred yuan to dozens of yuan, are countless. The total amount is estimated to be over 100,000 yuan. In addition to the above-mentioned individuals, Huang Houchu, the principal of Liuxi Elementary School, as well as three teachers and thirty-two students were kidnapped. However, the Tongchang Dried Goods store had pre-emptively piled a large number of sugar packages at the front and back doors. The bandits attacked for two or three hours, but still could not break in, so there was no damage at all.

Physiological Anomaly 118

▲ Farm Woman Infertile for Many Years

▲ Suddenly Produces Breast Milk

Lu, the 36-year-old wife of Huang Amao, a farmer from Huangjiazhai, about four miles southwest of Yangxing in Baoshan, has been married to Huang for eighteen years. When Lu was 24 years old (i.e., in 1918), she conceived and gave birth to a son, who unfortunately died before his first birthday. After Lu's grief, she developed an internal illness and has not conceived since. But last month, Lu's period suddenly stopped, and the whole family was overjoyed, believing that she was undoubtedly pregnant. Unexpectedly, Lu suddenly felt her breasts swelling and producing milk a few days ago, which greatly alarmed her. She told her husband, Huang Amao, who then consulted a doctor. But after the doctor diagnosed Lu, he found that she had no illness and verified that the liquid flowing from Lu's breasts was indeed milk. After the news spread, nearby farmers rushed to see it, all considering it a strange event. Soon after, a relative of Huang's, named Zhang, brought his three-month-old infant to Huang's house to be breastfed by Lu. The infant has been drinking the milk for a day and a night now, and the situation is quite good, with no signs of any problems. This kind of special physiological anomaly is truly remarkable.

The Kidnapped Owner of a Machine Factory Rescued from Danger 119

▲ Fourteen Men and Women Arrested

▲ Accomplices Captured in Zhabei

On the 25th of last month, over ten bandits armed with weapons broke into the home of Wang Shunjin, the owner of the Tongshengxing Machine Factory at No. 533 Gongping Road, Yangshupu. They first robbed him of 106 yuan in cash and then kidnapped Wang's three-year-old son, Xiasheng, and fled. After being robbed, the victim rushed to report to the police station and requested an investigation. The day before yesterday, detectives from the Huishan Police Station discovered that Wang's child was being held in a house at No. 644 Xinzha Road. Western and Chinese detectives armed with weapons rushed to surround the bandit's den, then entered and searched it. In addition to rescuing the hostage, they also captured fourteen individuals, including the bandits Jia Kuizhi, Li Zhaozhen, Yang Sihu, Chen Lidian, Chen Lilan, Wang Laowu, Ji Sha, Wang Jiajiu, Zhou Guanqing, Sun Chenghuai, Wang Maozheng, as well as Jia's wife, Jia Jiang, Zhou's wife, Zhou Shen, and Sun's wife, Sun Yuan. They were detained separately. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Special District Court, where Judge Feng Shide conducted the interrogation. Prevalence of Seasonal Diseases in Shanghai 120

▲ High Mortality Rates for Smallpox and Meningitis

The Ministry of Health cited the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau's spring report, which listed smallpox and epidemic meningitis as diseases with high mortality rates. The current season is the most prone to epidemics. The Ministry requested the Municipal Government to instruct the Health Bureau to strengthen preventive measures in order to prevent transmission. The Municipal Government then instructed the Health Bureau to comply. According to the Bureau's response, the smallpox patients discovered in the spring were entirely impoverished residents. The Bureau, aware of this, has launched city-wide smallpox vaccinations in the shantytowns. However, due to traditional customs, the common people are not receiving vaccinations in large numbers. Despite repeated explanations, progress is still difficult. As for the occurrence of epidemic meningitis, it is feared that it was introduced by carriers (those who carry infectious bacteria without showing symptoms). This is because the disease has already been epidemic in neighboring Songjiang, Baoshan, and other areas near Shanghai. Due to the heavy traffic in Shanghai, the occurrence of the disease due to carriers is unavoidable. In addition to promptly isolating patients with meningitis, the Bureau has also been distributing various leaflets about the disease at any time and injecting groups and individuals with meningitis preventive vaccines to prevent its spread and stop the epidemic.

Statistics on Infectious Diseases in February 121

Yesterday, the Municipal Health Bureau released the monthly report on statutory infectious diseases in Shanghai Special Municipality for February. There were 18 cases of typhoid or paratyphoid fever, 3 cases of dysentery, 15 cases of smallpox with 4 deaths, 33 cases of diphtheria with 4 deaths, 30 cases of epidemic meningitis with 7 deaths, and 21 cases of scarlet fever with 1 death. In total, there were 126 cases with 16 deaths.

New Regulations for Family Visits to Detainees in Civil Cases 125

▲ 10:00 AM to 12:00 PM

▲ 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM

Previously, the Civil Detention Center of the Special District Court limited family visits to civil defendants to the period from 2:00 PM to 4:30 PM daily. Now, the newly appointed Director, Xie Fuci, has revised these regulations, effective from the 7th of this month. A notice has been prepared and posted in front of the center, as follows: Notice regarding the matter of family visits. Family visits for civil detainees have always been scheduled from 2:00 PM to 4:30 PM, with openings every thirty minutes. However, this method has been quite chaotic when there are many people. Therefore, starting from the 7th of this month, the visiting hours will be re-regulated as follows: Anyone requesting a visit during these hours must register and will be allowed to visit upon arrival, for convenience and easier management. This notice is hereby issued for the information of all detainees and their families. Visiting hours are from 10:00 AM to 12:00 PM and from 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM. Visiting time must not exceed thirty minutes.

Major Theft, Robbery, Kidnapping, and Murder Cases Committed by Notorious Bandits 128

▲ Yesterday's Trial at the French Concession Court

▲ Each Bandit Sentenced Separately

The China-France Construction Company at No. 653 Xujiahui Road in the French Concession was previously broken into by bandits, who stole 4,500 yuan and fled. Afterwards, the French police paid special attention to this case and posted a reward for their arrest. The French police's special task force, consisting of detective inspector Jin Jiulin, detectives Wang Rusong, Li Yaolong, Qian Yumin, and informants Zhou Yaoting, Zhang Ziying, and Zhou Buguang, discovered the whereabouts of the notorious thieves Song Xiaoliuzi, also known as Song Zhenglou, and Chen Yonggui. They immediately went to arrest them. Song and Chen, as well as four accomplices, Wang San and Chen Asi, and the female thief Song Zeng, were all arrested. Two Mauser pistols, two handguns, and a pair of handcuffs were confiscated and taken to the police station. After further investigation, the detectives discovered that Song and his gang had previously robbed the home of Lin Zhou at No. 61 Tongkang Lane, Mintineiyin Road, the cigarette and paper store opened by Wang Fusheng at No. 353 Caishi Road, and the leather shoe store opened by Zhou Fukang on Luban Road. They also assassinated Wang Xinfa at No. 149 Mintineiyin Road last year, kidnapped Zhang Zukang, who lived at No. 379 Mayerxi'ai Road in the French Concession, and hid him in the Caojiadu area. They had also committed multiple kidnapping and assassination cases in the Public Concession. After the police chief provided detailed confessions, the men were sent to the French court yesterday for trial. First, Western Inspector Sachiel presented the situation, along with the handguns and Mauser pistols. Then, the plaintiffs, Wang Fusheng, Zhou Fukang, Wang Linpei, and the woman Lin Zhou, filed complaints about the robbery. Song Xiaoliuzi confessed that he was from Jiangbei, 33 years old, and had been working as a laborer. In October of the previous year, Wang Are, who was at large, initiated the robbery at No. 61 Tongkang Lane. On December 20 of the previous year, Jin Changfa initiated the robbery at the cigarette and paper store on Caishi Road, obtaining 60 yuan. On July 2 of the previous year, Wang Linfa asked civilians to avenge his foster father, Liu Lianghong, and assassinated Wang Xinfa upstairs at No. 149 Mintineiyin Road. Afterwards, Wang Linfa gave each of them 50 yuan. On December 30 of the previous year, Wang Laowu, Jin Laosan, and others initiated the robbery at the China-France Company, obtaining over 4,000 yuan. Afterwards, each civilian received 500 yuan. On February 11 of this year, they robbed the leather shoe store opened by Zhou Fukang on Luban Road. On March 16, he was arrested by the police. Chen Yonggui confessed that he was from Zhenjiang and had been a tailor for the Hongbang gang. On February 11, Wang Laowu asked civilians to go to the leather shoe store on Luban Road to rob it. Afterwards, each civilian received 5 yuan. He knew nothing about the other cases. Wang San confessed that Song Xiaoliuzi had brought the handgun to him to hide, wrapped in paper, so he did not know it was a dangerous item. Chen Asi confessed that someone surnamed someone he knew had told him about the kidnapping of Zhang Zukang, but he was not actually present at the scene. Song Zeng confessed that her husband, Song Xiaoliuzi, was a thief outside, which she knew nothing about, and asked for leniency. Judge Zhu Cheng obtained the confession and, with the approval of French Consul Duna, sentenced Song Xiaoliuzi and Chen Yonggui each to five years in a Western prison and deportation, to be handed over to the mainland authorities for trial. Chen Yonggui will be sent to the Public Concession for questioning first. Wang San will be imprisoned for three years and deported, then sent to the Public Concession for questioning. Chen Asi will be sent to the Public Concession for questioning. Song Zeng will be permanently deported. The handguns and Mauser pistols seized in the case will be confiscated.

Pirates Rampage Outside Wusong Port Again 129

At around 7:00 PM the night before last, over thirty large sand boats filled with pirates suddenly arrived at Lusi Port outside Wusong Port. They immediately began to loot the merchant ships anchored in the port, sparing none. They then proceeded to land and attack the local Public Security Bureau to seize firearms. Because the bandits came suddenly and were outnumbered, they were unable to resist. As a result, all the firearms were seized by the bandits, increasing their power. They then proceeded to search the shops and homes of the residents. After receiving the report, Director Wu of the Wusong Maritime Patrol immediately dispatched the Jingxing and Yisheng gunboats to suppress the pirates. Zhu Bingzheng, the district chief of the water police, has also dispatched the 17th Brigade to intercept them.

City Ferry Prohibits Carrying Flammable Goods 130

▲ Limit of Ten Packages for Cotton Textiles

Yesterday, the Shanghai Special Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities issued a notice stating, "This is a notice regarding the matter that the Bureau has previously announced a ban on the transportation of bulk goods on city ferries. This is because city ferries are primarily for passenger transport, and the transportation of flammable goods is restricted by the water insurance regulations, which is unavoidable. The intention is to maintain the safety of both the ferry itself and the passengers and goods. However, it is inconvenient to ban passengers from carrying cotton textiles, such as lace, which they rely on for clothing and food, when traveling on the ferry. After consulting with the insurance company, an agreement has been reached to allow a limited number of such items to be carried, but each trip will be limited to ten packages. The packages must be tightly wrapped to prevent them from catching fire easily. Goods that are easily flammable, such as cotton, are still prohibited from being carried. This notice is hereby issued for public information."
