Tenants' Meeting in Jingyi Lane 133

All the tenants of Jingyi Lane, Bailaini Mengma Road, French Concession, held a meeting at the Nanyang Bridge Chamber of Commerce yesterday at 9 PM, due to the landlord's unwarranted demolition. The following resolutions were made: (1) If the landlord agrees not to force tenants to move out, the tenants will be ready to pay the outstanding rent, but there must be adequate security; (2) If the landlord incurs losses due to house repairs, water rate increases, etc., a comprehensive calculation can be made. If there are indeed losses, the tenants are also willing to moderately increase the rent; (3) If the landlord insists that the tenants must move out, the tenants will suffer huge losses, estimated at over 300 yuan per household. If the landlord can compensate for the losses, the tenants will reluctantly make a final concession; (4) If the landlord does not follow the above three methods, all the tenants will, no matter how oppressed, vow not to move; (5) The current representative of the landlord, Zhang Xingbei, and the tenants publicly request the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, Xu Xiuting, to mediate. All tenants are awaiting the fair judgment of the two representatives. The final decision rests with all the tenants. The above methods were put to a vote by the chairman and passed unanimously. The meeting adjourned at 11 PM.

Six Batches of New Houses to be Built on Avenue Edward VII 134

From the houses along the northern frontage of Avenue Edward VII, east of Baxianqiao, French Concession, to the Gongguan Road near Zhengjia Muqiao Waitou, except for a few newly built houses inside, most of the others, such as Bulinde, Shande, Dongxi Gaodi, and Gaoyang Lanes, consisting of hundreds of buildings, are dilapidated. The landlords have unanimously decided to rebuild them all into the latest-style three-story market houses. All businesses have been notified to move out within a specified period. Shops and residents have been moving out successively. As of yesterday, they have all been barricaded, and large-scale construction will commence immediately. It is estimated that they will be completed in half a year.

Two Suspects in Murder Case Found to Have No Illegal Activities 135

▲ Wang Daliu Granted Bail

▲ Ye Deqing Released Without Charge

Wang Daliu (also known as Mao Yubo) and Ye Deqing, Jiangbei natives and cooks in the workshop of the Gungda Cotton Mill on Huasheng Road, Yangshupu, were reported to the Municipal Police Bureau by Ye Kesong as the murderers who shot Lin Wenhan in Taixing County, Jiangbei, on November 18th last year. The bureau dispatched detectives to work with the relevant police station, and Wang and Ye were temporarily detained for interrogation. A long time has passed, and there has been no official request for extradition from Taixing County. According to the police station's investigation, the two men have been working in the Gungda workshop for quite some time and have no history of illegal activities. Moreover, Wang Daliu has never used the name Mao Yubo. Yesterday morning, Judge Feng Shide of the Special District Local Court held a hearing. After hearing the reports from Chinese and foreign detectives, Ye Kesong insisted in court that Wang Daliu was indeed the murderer present at the scene and that Taixing County had already issued an arrest warrant. As for Ye Deqing, he was not present at the scene. Wang Daliu denied being Mao Yubo and claimed that he had been working as a cook in the Shanghai cotton mill workshop for a long time, had never left Shanghai, and had never murdered Lin Wenhan. Ye also denied any illegal activities. The lawyers representing the two defendants presented their defense. After reviewing the evidence, the judge ordered Wang Daliu to be released on bail provided by a shop and released Ye Deqing without charge.

Case of Murdering Patrolman to be Tried Jointly 136

Liu Youqing, Chinese patrolman No. 463 of the Gordon Road Police Station, was shot and killed by robbers on the night of the 31st of last month while pursuing them. Subsequently, Detective Chang Xihuan of the police station arrested four suspects in Zhabei. One of them, Wang Xiaoguozi, has already been handed over to the Special District Local Court for trial. The remaining three are still detained at the Public Security Bureau, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. The three detained at the Public Security Bureau are named Liu Siwangzi, Shi Zhaoqing, and Yao Gongxing, all from Jiangbei. The day before yesterday afternoon, Detective Chang went to the Public Security Bureau and brought the three men back to the police station. After investigation, it was found that Shi and Yao had no connection with the robbery and assault case. Yesterday morning, they were taken to the Special District Local Court, where Judge Wu Tingqi held a hearing. The police station's lawyer requested that the charges against Shi and Yao be dropped and that Liu be detained to be tried jointly with Wang Xiaoguozi. Judge Wu granted the request, ordered Liu to be returned to custody, and released Shi and Yao.

Private Torture by Hanging 137

▲ Is Chen Ruzhen a Detective?

▲ Wei Guoan Wrongfully Accused

Wei Guoan, 27 years old, from Wuxian, who used to weave silk, lives in Jiande New Village, Sanyang Road, Zhabei. On the evening of March 28th, Zhou Dazhen's house, No. 10 in front of Wei's residence, was reported to have had five or six pieces of clothing stolen. The next day, the incident was reported to the local Public Security Bureau sub-station for investigation. Suddenly, a man claiming to be a detective named Chen Ruzhen, suspecting Wei Guoan, arrested Wei and subjected him to various forms of private torture, resulting in injuries all over his body. However, Wei consistently denied the accusations. The detective had no choice but to release Wei and send him home. Having suffered this humiliation, Wei hired lawyer Wu Deyuan and filed a lawsuit with the Shanghai Local Court Prosecutor's Office, accusing Chen Ruzhen, Zhou Dazhen, and others of falsely accusing him of theft and subjecting him to private torture. The court approved the request, and yesterday ordered the judicial police to bring Chen Ruzhen, Zhou Dazhen, and others to the court for a preliminary hearing, along with the plaintiff Wei Guoan. After the investigation, the prosecutor determined that Chen Ruzhen did indeed commit private torture by hanging. Chen Ruzhen was immediately detained and taken into custody pending prosecution. Zhou Dazhen and the plaintiff Wei Guoan were dismissed and instructed to await further summons.

Maid Suffocated by Coal Gas 138

Wang Yangshi, a maid from Anhui, 34 years old, employed by a certain family at No. 31 Qingfu Lane, Pushi Road, French New Concession, burned a coal briquette stove in her room on the night of the 1st of this month to keep warm because of the cold weather. Unexpectedly, she was poisoned by the coal gas. Yangshi and her cousin, Hangshi, who shared the room, were suffocated and moaning. The employer noticed and immediately reported to the police station. The two women were taken to Renji Hospital. Hangshi suffered less poisoning and was rescued. Yangshi, due to severe poisoning, was not saved and died the day before yesterday. The hospital notified the police station, and the body was taken to the Tongren Fuyuantang morgue for examination. Yesterday, the police station reported to Judge Zhu of the French Court, who inspected the body and confirmed that the deceased had indeed been suffocated by coal gas. The employer was ordered to prepare a coffin for the burial.

Kidnapper Zhang Yingtang Granted Extradition 139

Detectives from the Shanghai Special Municipality Public Security Bureau reported to the French Police Station the day before yesterday that a kidnapper named Zhang Yingtang had previously colluded with accomplices to kidnap someone in the interior, extorting a large sum of money and sharing the spoils. After the case was exposed, he fled and was now under their jurisdiction. They requested assistance in arresting him. The police chief ordered detectives to cooperate and arrest Zhang. Yesterday, he was escorted to the French Court for questioning. The detectives first stated the details of the case and requested extradition. Zhang confessed that he knew about the case but was not present at the time. He admitted to spending thirty yuan. The detectives further claimed that Zhang had actually received six hundred yuan. The Chinese and foreign judges approved the extradition of the defendant for further investigation.

Country Boy Standing by the Road Causes Accident 141

▲ Injured by Car

Chen Ziquan, 526 years old (likely a typo, should be 52 or 26), from Chuansha, accompanied his son A'nan, 13 years old, and daughter Xiaomei yesterday morning at 9:00 AM from the Beihuo Railway Station Hanqiao to Jielu to wait for a tram, then to the Putan Copper Man Wharf to take a ferry to a long-distance bus home. At that time, it was when the Nanjing bus arrived, and people and vehicles were extremely crowded. A'nan, a country boy, only knew how to watch the excitement and play, without knowing the dangers. A cargo truck from a certain company, fully loaded with goods, was turning onto North Zhejiang Road. Seeing the country boy standing, the driver honked the horn repeatedly. However, A'nan ignored it. The driver braked urgently, but it was too late, and A'nan was knocked down, losing consciousness. The patrolling police arrived and sent the injured A'nan to the relevant police station, which ordered him to be sent to the General Hospital for treatment. Doctors found that A'nan's ankle bone was broken, and it is feared that one foot will be disabled.

Municipal Government Encourages Construction of Affordable Housing 143

▲ Guarantee of 80% of Rent ▲ Request for Commendation

The Affordable Housing Construction Committee of this city, in order to promote the construction of affordable housing, drafted incentive measures, which were approved by the municipal government yesterday. The articles are as follows: (Article 1) Any individual or organization that builds affordable housing in accordance with the following items shall be entitled to the benefits stipulated in these measures: (1) The construction site must be designated or approved by this government; (2) There must be at least one hundred rooms, but this does not apply to those who add to existing buildings on the same site; (3) The housing shall be rented to slum dwellers designated by this government first; (4) The rent for the housing shall be approved by this government; (5) The management and leasing rules shall be submitted to this government for approval; (6) The demolition or change of use of the housing shall be at least ten years later, unless approved by this government. (Article 2) Builders of affordable housing shall report the following items to this government: (1) The name and address of the owner. If the housing is built on leased land, the name and address of the landlord and the lease agreement shall also be reported; (2) A site map (detailing the construction site); (3) Building plans and construction details (detailing the number of rooms, layout, construction materials, and various facilities); (4) The cost of construction, land price or land rent, and other equipment costs, and the estimated rent. (Article 3) Builders of affordable housing may apply to this government to choose one of the following methods: (1) This government will rent all the housing and sublet it to the public. The owner will still be responsible for the cost of housing repairs.

This is to express our deep gratitude. Establishment of Police Station at Yujidun to Dredge the River 146

Yujidun in West Shanghai is located on the upper reaches of the Wusong River. The river section is extremely silted, and it is a necessary area for various commercial and cargo ships on the inland river. Congestion and breakages often occur, especially for rice boats, which are most affected. Each time there is a breakage and dredging, it costs a lot of manpower and money, often taking more than ten days to pass. The Shanghai Special Municipality Public Security Bureau Water Patrol Team has now established a police station at this place, with two patrol chiefs, Wang and Tian, and more than twenty police officers stationed in the Yuji Temple, specializing in dredging the river and managing traffic. In addition, since there are no pedestrians in the area after sunset, and gunshots are sometimes heard, it is extremely desolate and dangerous. In order to maintain the safety and tranquility of merchants and travelers, the Public Security Bureau will raise funds in the second half of the year to build police housing on Yujidun to expand its strength in order to have a high vantage point and comprehensive defense. A few days ago, the river section from Jiwang Temple to Zhangjiajing was again blocked. Patrol Chiefs Wang and Tian supervised eight police officers and worked hard to dredge it. Traffic has now been restored. Therefore, in the past two days, the number of rice boats arriving in the city from the north has slightly increased, totaling more than one hundred, and the price of rice has fallen by several cents as a result.

Urgent Appeal from Henan Province for Disaster Relief 147

Zhou Xiwenzhou, the representative of the Henan Provincial Relief Association stationed in Shanghai, received an urgent telegram from the association yesterday. The telegram reads as follows: "To the Relief Associations of Various Provinces: We have recently sent a telegram to the Central Government, the Executive Yuan, and the Relief Commission, which reads: 'To the Executive Committee of the Nanjing Central Party Headquarters, the Chairman of the National Government Chiang, the Heads of the various Yuan, the Ministers of the various Ministries, and the Chairman of the Relief Commission Xu Jun: The disaster in Henan is severe, deaths are continuing, and disaster relief funds are urgently needed. Our association has repeatedly appealed in telegrams, but the Ministry of Finance says that there are no more treasury bills left and cannot continue to allocate funds, and the disaster relief bonds have no source of funds and cannot be issued. The bad news has been received, and millions of disaster victims are crying in unison. The reason why the revolutionary government calls on the people and the people support the revolutionary government is that the government relieves the suffering of the people. The most painful thing for the people is starvation. Looking around Henan, there have been years of drought and floods, which have affected the entire province. Repeated wars have devastated more than fifty counties. During the spring famine, the poor and the rich are all in despair, dying in their hometowns and collapsing on the roads, numbering in the hundreds every day. More than tens of thousands of disaster victims have gathered in Xia, Luo, Zheng, and Bian, but there is no food for accommodation and no money for resettlement. We are deeply afraid that desperation will lead to unrest and that the situation will become unmanageable. Our association lacks the resources to provide relief and is deeply worried. The provincial treasury is empty and cannot raise funds. Treasury bills and bonds are not being issued. Our good compatriots are left to die and perish without any assistance. We hope that our government will not do this. We earnestly request you to allocate more funds and clearly indicate a solution. Millions of disaster victims are enduring death in the hope. Our hearts are in pain, and our words are direct. Please take note.' We ask for a unified call to allocate more funds for disaster relief. We are deeply grateful. Zhang Fang of the Henan Provincial Relief Association bows."

New Zhong Code Free Trial Method 151

The New Zhong Code Complete Book saves more than 30% on telegraph transmission costs and saves time and effort in decoding. It is a necessity for offices. Yesterday, the publishers announced a trial method in order to promote wide sales: Companies and institutions in this city can send a letter with a stamped seal to request a trial. The book will be sent to you and the payment will be collected five days later. If it is not suitable, the original book will be taken back and no money will be charged. For cities outside of this city, the book fee of one yuan and the registration fee of six cents must be remitted first. The book will be sent by registered mail. If it is not suitable, the original book must be returned within five days, and the book fee and original remittance will be returned. The publisher is the New Zhong Engineering Company, located at No. 7 Ningbo Road. This kind of free trial method is common in the European and American publishing industry, so it is trusted and avoids readers spending money on unsuitable books. It is an innovation in our country. It is heard that the book is sold in the Shanghai Commercial Press, Radio Bureau, and China Telegraph Bureau for one yuan each, and many people have adopted it.

Fire in a Shack in Pudong 152

A Shandong man named Cai Bing'er had built a shack near the cigarette factory road in Lujiazui, Pudong, to roast and sell peanuts. At 4:00 AM the other day, the roof of the shack was accidentally set on fire, and the flames spread rapidly, burning everything down in an instant. Cai woke up from his sleep in shock, but luckily escaped quickly, avoiding disaster. Afterwards, a patrol officer from the Fourth Squad of the police arrested Cai and sent him to the Third District Public Security Bureau, where he was fined three yuan and ordered not to build another shack to prevent danger.

Overview of the Venue 155

Yesterday was the fourth day of the National Games. The competitions and publicity of the previous three days had attracted the attention of society as a whole. Therefore, despite the cloudy weather, there weren't many spectators in the morning, as everyone knew that the important finals were in the afternoon. After noon, there was heavy traffic in front of the venue, which soon became crowded, and all the seats were filled. Many men and women came from afar to Hangzhou to watch the games. The scene was no less grand than the opening day. The situation of yesterday is recorded below:

▲Visiting Groups

Yesterday, in addition to those who purchased tickets to enter the venue, there were the following groups who came to visit: Anhui Girls' Middle School (30 people), Henan Women's Vocational School (5 people), Central University (15 people), Pudong Middle School (100 people), Taicang Middle School (50 people), Wuxi Middle School (15 people), Liaoning Tonghua Education Group (5 people), Xuzhou Middle School (400 people), Central Military Training Brigade (850 people), Shanghai East Asia Physical Education College (100 people), Liangjiang Physical Education College (100 people), Suzhou Chenglie Physical Education College (15 people), Chengdu University (19 people), Jimei Women's Vocational School (14 people), Kindergarten Normal School (27 people), and 42 schools and organizations from various cities and counties in this province, totaling approximately 29,800 people.

▲Number of Tickets Sold

The number of tickets sold at the entrances and exits of each venue on the third day was 1,068 for the track and field stadium, with a ticket price of 1,763 jiao; 770 for the basketball court, with a ticket price of 1,546 jiao; 11 for the tennis court, with a ticket price of 22 jiao; and 52 for the general admission tickets, with a ticket price of 104 yuan, totaling 1,901 tickets and a total ticket price of 381 yuan.

▲Traffic and Publicity

Since the entrances and exits of each venue were reorganized, the order has been further improved. The military police have maintained order throughout. The organizing committee also printed and distributed a map of the entrances and exits of the venue for the convenience of spectators. All the routes to each venue are marked on the map, allowing people to easily find their way around without having to wander back and forth, which was greatly appreciated. The various news items published in the official program were also praised by the audience. They were distributed in the venue early in the morning, so that people could get a comprehensive overview of the day's competition results.

▲Mr. Chen's Visit

For this National Games, each provincial and municipal government sent important officials as representatives to participate in Hangzhou. The Jiangsu Provincial Government originally appointed Chen Hexian, the Director of Education, as its representative, but the opening day coincided with the inauguration of the Jiangsu Provincial Government Committee members, so Chen was unable to come to Hangzhou. He visited the Games on the fourth day and expressed great satisfaction with the various arrangements. Chen also plans to stay longer to see the entire Games.

▲Dedicated Staff

Although the organizing committee staff have been working day and night for days, they are full of energy and show no signs of fatigue. The president and vice president, Dai Jitao and Zhang Renjie, as well as the director and deputy director of the preparatory committee, Zhu Jiahua and Zhou Xiangxian, are all very enthusiastic. In addition to handling all kinds of affairs, they also visit each venue. The organizing committee staff also arrive on time to work, so that the internal and external affairs are handled in a well-organized and orderly manner.

Football Second Round 173

(1) Nanjing Wins Big Over Hunan Nine to Two

(2) Liaoning Wins Over Tianjin Three to One

▲The Nanjing-Hunan Game

The first match of the second round was between Nanjing and Hunan. Not long after the start of the game, the Nanjing team launched a fierce attack on the opponent, and the Hunan inner defender slipped, but fortunately the goalkeeper saved the goal. Hunan was extremely lucky to not lose this ball. For about ten minutes, the two sides were in a stalemate. Later, Jiang Zhihong, the right winger of Nanjing, made many excellent crosses, but unfortunately the center forward's shots were inaccurate and all failed. Once, Liu Zukan, the left winger, took a corner kick, and the ball landed in a good spot. The center forward rushed up to head the ball, but it went over the crossbar, which was a great pity. Seeing that the situation was not good, the Hunan team tried to counterattack, but the Nanjing team's inner defenders were very strong, and the Hunan forwards could not cross the line. Thirty minutes later, Liu Zukan, the left winger of Nanjing, dribbled the ball along the sideline and went straight in. At the appropriate position, the pass went over the head of the Hunan defender, and the Nanjing right inner forward calmly shot the ball in. After that, the Nanjing team successively shot two goals into the enemy's goal, but both were disallowed because of offside. At that time, the Hunan team was still recovering from the shock when the inner defender Deng Shuchu slipped another goal in. Then, the Nanjing right inner forward dribbled the ball straight in and scored another goal. After scoring the third goal, the Nanjing team's momentum increased even more. Finally, the right inner forward and the left winger successively dribbled in two more goals. The first half ended with a score of five to zero. Switching sides and fighting again, the Nanjing team had a strong momentum in the first ten minutes. With the help of Ling Yuanyang, the left winger Liu Zukan scored a goal. The Hunan team bucked up and also scored a goal. Soon after, the Nanjing right inner forward, with the assistance of the right winger, kicked in a goal. At twenty minutes, a certain Nanjing inner defender fouled in the twelve-yard area, and the Hunan center forward Fang kicked the ball into the net. In the last five minutes, the Nanjing team's Zhong Guanming and Ling Yuanyang scored two more goals. The final result was nine to two, and Nanjing won.

The reason for the Hunan team's defeat was that the whole team could not cooperate, and they were extremely flustered when receiving the ball, sometimes crowding together in one place, and sometimes retreating. As a result, the Nanjing team was able to attack continuously. However, the Nanjing team's shooting accuracy was lacking, otherwise the opponent's loss would have been even greater. The referee was Tang Zhongguang. The lineups of the two teams are listed on the left:

Nanjing Team: Tan Zhongzhang, Yu Mianchu, Gu Shuxun, Ling Huiyang, Gao Limin, Gu Yuanliang, Zhong Guanming, Ling Yuanyang, Liu Zukan, Jiang Zhihong

Positions: Goalkeeper, Right Back, Left Back, Center Back, Right Midfielder, Left Midfielder, Center Forward, Left Inner Forward, Right Inner Forward, Left Winger, Right Winger

Hunan Team: Li Guoji, Zou Shuzeng, Xie Jixian, Sun Ming, Xiang Shaoyi, You Shaoze, Chen Jiaying, Zhu Baofeng, Liu Xingheng, Wang Zidai, Zhou Shu'an

▲The Fierce Battle Between Liaoning and Tianjin

The football match between Liaoning and Tianjin was a battle between two strong teams. The outcome of this match was very important for the finals, so the two sides fought extremely fiercely. The Liaoning forwards were all strong and brave, and the team's coordination was good. In particular, the two inner defenders and the center back were commendable for their interception. Their passing can also be said to have reached a high level. On the Tianjin side, they had more courage than wisdom, which was a major reason for their failure. In terms of the team's overall skills, their defense was better than their offense. Sun Guilin, the left midfielder, was a rare talent for his interception and counterattack, making it difficult for the Liaoning team's forwards to move. In the previous match between the Tianjin team and the Zhejiang team, Sun played very well as the left inner forward, but today he played as the left midfielder, which greatly affected the forwards. After a bitter battle in the first half, each side scored one goal. In the second half, the Tianjin team's formation faltered, and Wu Gongrong, the left forward of Liaoning, scored a goal. Soon after, Liu Bao, the left winger, scored another goal. As a result, Liaoning won by a score of three to one.

▲The Situation of Kobe's Victory Over Hubei

The Kobe team sent back to the country

The Kobe Overseas Chinese basketball team, in view of the fact that overseas Chinese elsewhere have sent teams back to the country to serve, such as the baseball team from Honolulu and the basketball team from the Philippines, etc., while Japan alone had none, felt very regrettable. This time, the unprecedented National Games were held in Hangzhou, with participants from 22 provinces and cities. The number of athletes was the largest ever, bringing together the best athletes from across the country to compete and learn from each other. Upon hearing the news, the Japanese Overseas Chinese did not hesitate to spend a lot of money to send the Kobe Overseas Chinese basketball team back to the country to participate in the grand event and promote it. The

Zheng Fenghualan, First in Women's High Jump, Breaks National Record Photo by Xie Yuexi 175

team has been in Hangzhou for six days, and finally made its debut yesterday, making people eager to see them. The spectators were enthusiastic, and the area around the venue was already completely crowded, which shows the excitement.

Xiao Meizhen, Second in Women's High Jump Photo by Xie Yuexi 176

Zhao Wenzhao (Right), First in the Discus Throw, and Zhang Shi'an (Left), Second Photo by Xie Yuexi 177

Ranked Third in Japan 178

The Kobe Overseas Chinese basketball team is called "V-Fly" and is one of the strongest teams in Kobe. It has won the Kobe basketball league championship for several years in a row and has never encountered an opponent. Westerners also participate in the Kobe basketball championship, and strong teams such as K.R.&A.C. and the Canadian Academy are often defeated by them. The All-Japan Basketball Championship is divided into the Kansai and Kanto regions. The Kanto region has more universities, so it is stronger than the Kansai region. Kobe belongs to the Kansai region, and the Overseas Chinese basketball team also participates in the competition. This championship is held once a year. Last year, the team played against the Kansai Gakuin in the final for the championship. Because of unfair officiating, they lost by only one point and finished as the runner-up. This year, they played two friendly matches against the Kansai Gakuin again and won both times. The score of the second match was seventy-one to forty-four, a very large difference. On the night before returning to China, the Osaka Basketball Club sent a letter requesting a match. The team won again with a score of fifty-six to twenty. Their strength is strong and they dominate Japan. They can be ranked third in all of Japan.

The Hubei Team is the Essence of Central China 179

Hubei basketball is the essence of Central China. In the Central China Games, the athletes from Wuhan won every match, and their skills were the best in all provinces. This time, they came from afar with the intention of competing against the teams from the North and South. One is the king of overseas, and the other is the hegemon of Central China, so there should be a fierce competition.

Yesterday's Game Was Very Worth Watching 180

At 1:00 PM, the referee slowly arrived at the venue. The whistle sounded and the battle began. The Kobe team wore bright red vests with yellow V's, and the Hubei team wore black vests with white letters, looking exceptionally valiant. Kobe took the lead, with Xu Chenghao passing the ball to the right forward Lei Huiwang, and the "Little Thunder" scored with a quick shot, opening the score. Xu Shengtong then scored two more goals in a row. Suffering this heavy blow, Hubei tried hard to recover, and Peng Shuchu and Yuan Qingwu also scored successively. Before long, the Kobe forwards displayed their prowess. Xu Shengtong's shots were almost always successful. Hubei made some gains, but the difference was already too great to catch up. The result of the first half was forty-eight to nineteen, and Kobe won.

Men's Volleyball

Second Round: Fujian Wins Against Tianjin 185

▲A Score of 2 to 0

▲Fujian's Strength is Great

The Fujian volleyball team has long enjoyed a great reputation in South China, with a continuous stream of talented players. The team participating in this competition is composed of the elite players from the province, possessing formidable strength. The Tianjin team has long been renowned in North China and can be considered a strong force. They showed their skills in the preliminary rounds, and the audience praised them endlessly. At 9:00 AM on the 4th, the two teams met in the second round, and those in the know already anticipated a fierce competition. At the sound of the clock striking nine and the referee's whistle, the athletes of both teams braced themselves, attacking and defending, each showing their strengths. At the start of the match, Fujian was extremely strong. Cheng Qiaosheng, Weng Zulie, Liao Dengru, and Zhang Qiushen served the ball, scoring eleven consecutive points. The Tianjin team tried hard to resist but made no progress, which was unexpected by the audience. However, during the intense battle, there were many exciting performances. The reason for Tianjin's defeat was indeed poor coordination. Under such a strong enemy, trying to succeed by luck was naturally difficult. It was not a failure of strategy but a lack of strength. After changing sides, the Tianjin team showed some activity, scoring five points successively. However, Fujian's momentum was strong and unstoppable. In the end, they lost with a score of 5 to 21. In the second game, Tianjin's formation was excellent, with strong blocking in the front row and effective defense in the back row. The scores were consistently close, giving hope for a comeback. Unfortunately, at 13 to 14, they were repeatedly attacked by Fujian and limited by the surrounding circumstances. The Fujian team's offense and defense were effective, repeatedly achieving success, and the score gradually increased. They won the second game with a score of 21 to 13, resulting in a final score of 2 to 0. Referee: Tan Tianpei; The lineups of the two teams are listed on the left:

▲The Battle Between Guangdong and Shanghai

The second round of the volleyball championship between Guangdong and Shanghai B took place at 1:00 PM on the 4th. The Guangdong team has profound volleyball skills and a resounding reputation in South China. In this women's volleyball competition, they have a solid hope of winning the championship. The Shanghai B team is also a rising star, having defeated the strong Jiangsu team in the preliminary rounds, which was highly praised. Therefore, more than 1,000 people, attracted by the reputation of the two teams, went to watch the match, crowding both sides of the stands and creating an extremely lively atmosphere. At the start of the match, the two teams were evenly matched for the first few plays. The Guangdong team became increasingly brave as they fought, and the players were extremely agile, jumping and returning the ball with great skill. Shanghai B tried their best to resist but gradually felt overwhelmed. Their serves were powerful and their spikes were swift, surpassing even those of men. Compared to the strength of Shanghai B, the difference was too great. In less than ten minutes, they lost the first game with a score of 21 to 2. After continuing the battle, they continued to lose. From beginning to end, Shanghai B made no progress and eventually lost again with a score of 21 to 4. Judging from the situation of the match, the Guangdong team indeed had amazing skills. Looking at the participating teams, only Shanghai A could compete with them, while the others were difficult to match. Referee: Qiu Jixiang; The lineups are listed below:

A Brief Review of Yesterday's Athletics Competition 192

Yesterday was the final day of the men's and women's athletics competitions. The competition between Shanghai and Liaoning for the athletics championship was extremely intense. The audience was also more crowded and excited than the previous two days. Here is a brief description of the various finals:

▲200 Meters

The men's 200-meter final was held at 2:00 PM yesterday. The intense competition between the sprinters from the North and South was no less than that of yesterday's 100 meters. At the start of the race, Liu Changchun reversed his attitude from the previous few days, starting very quickly. He was in first place from start to finish. When he reached the finish line, he was about ten steps ahead of Zhong Lianji. The result was also quite good, proving that Liu had put in a lot of effort. Zhou Zhaoyuan of Tianjin was almost as fast as Liu in the first 100 meters. Zhong of Shanghai fell to third place, about one meter behind. By the finish line, Zhong had only surpassed Zhou by a shoulder, which was close.

▲800 Meters

In yesterday's 800-meter final, Deng Zhiming of Shanghai made a special effort and achieved a result of 2 minutes and 9 seconds, matching the national record set by Wang Xuanji, which was not easy. He was in the lead from start to finish. Lang Daikui of Liaoning was in fifth place at the start. Although he fought hard later, he finished second in the last half lap. When he was about 30 meters from the finish line, Lang desperately tried to catch up, but Deng Zhiming was already far ahead by ten steps, and there was no way to catch him.

▲Low Hurdles

In yesterday's men's low hurdles final, Cheng Jingguan of Jiangsu was in the lead at the start. Wang Yuzhen of Beiping and Liang Jingping of Guangdong followed closely. At around 120 meters, Liang of Guangdong started to run fast, leaping over the hurdles like flying, far surpassing Wang Yuzhen and Cheng Jingguan. Cheng had already fallen to second place. The result was 25.4 seconds, breaking the national record of 26.8 seconds set by Huang Jin in the 1929 North China Games, which was an outstanding result for the competition.

▲Women's 50 Meters

In the women's 50-meter final yesterday afternoon, Sun Guiyun, a female hero, immediately stood out and steadily won the championship. Liu Youqing and Huang Shuwei of Guangdong were also quite strong. If they work harder, they have a promising future. The result was 7.25 seconds, breaking the national record of 7.9 seconds held by Li Suiyin.

▲Women's 100 Meters

In yesterday's women's 100-meter final, Sun Guiyun was still in first place, and Liu Youqing was in second place. The distance between them was quite large, and there was no competition to speak of. The result was 13.8 seconds, breaking the record of 14.5 seconds set by Tong Jingbo in the 1929 North China Games.

▲10,000 Meters

Zhao Dexin Gallops Ahead

Setting a New National Record

Result: 35 Minutes, 36 Seconds and 1/5

Sixteen people participated in the 10,000-meter final. There were many good athletes, which attracted a lot of attention. Zhao Dexin of Liaoning, a famous long-distance runner from the Northeast, started leading after the first 1,000 meters, running ahead with steady steps from beginning to end. In the last 100 meters, he relied on his natural energy to surge forward, greatly increasing his speed, setting a new record of 35 minutes, 36 seconds and 1/5, which was commendable. Chen Xuzhou of Shanghai was also a good athlete, and he did his best yesterday, but due to his physique, he could not compete with the athletes from other places.

Triple Jump First Place Situ Guang, Photo by Xie Yuexi 193

▲Pole Vault

The pole vault final was quite competitive. Fu Baolu of Dongte won first place with 3.28 meters, a good result. Fu is a handsome young man, and he did not reach his best result yesterday. Li Lin of Shanghai failed to qualify at 3.17 meters, which was a pity. Otherwise, Shanghai would have had a chance to win the athletics championship.

▲Javelin Throw

In the javelin throw final, the result was 44 meters. Pan Nanshun won first place, which was very close to the national record. Yang Chuntai of Tianjin was initially in first place with 42.98 meters, but Pan surpassed him with 44.52 meters on his first attempt.

▲Women's Long Jump

In the women's long jump final, Wu Meixian of Dongte won first place with 4 meters. Xie Kuidi and Liu Youqing of Guangdong tied for second place with 3.96 meters. Wang Zhizhong of Tianjin won fourth place. Sun Guiyun of Dongte failed to qualify because she had competed in the 50-meter and 100-meter races consecutively.

Worthy of the True Colors of Athletes 194

Liu Changchun and Sun Guiyun

Liu Changchun, a male athlete from Liaoning, and Sun Guiyun, a female athlete from Dongte, have been the focus of attention since the opening of the competition. Liu won first place again in the 200-meter final yesterday (4th) at 1:00 PM, and Ms. Sun's result in the 50-meter final also exceeded her peers. As a result, the admiration for Liu and Sun has increased even more. Liu is usually straightforward, kind, and approachable. Although the athletes participating in this National Games compete against each other in sports, their feelings are still very harmonious because of Liu's attitude. Ms. Sun not only convinces people with her results but also inspires unity and the pursuit of progress with her gentle and courageous attitude. After yesterday's 50-meter final, she sat in the center of the field with Ms. Huang Shuwei of Guangdong and Ms. Cheng Enci of Nanjing to discuss sports for 20 minutes. When it came to important issues, such as the starting posture, she spoke in a dignified and loud voice. During the conversation, she would hold people's hands with her own and lean her head on their arms. Her attitude was truly remarkable. The French physical educationist Daos said in a speech at the National Stadium, "Athletes who have results but no attitude need to work harder." If Daos were at the scene, I believe he would have cheered and praised them as well.

Therefore, those who visit the event all praise and admire them and yearn to admire their charm, learn about their history, and understand their experiences after engaging in sports. We hereby send a letter to each participating team, requesting them to record and send the names and photos of each athlete, as well as the athletes' brief history and insights on the study of sports, to the group so that they can be published in the daily journal of the competition and published in other compiled works. In this way, those who are enlightened can enlighten others, allowing people across the country to learn from and emulate them,

Random Jottings 198

▲ Exorbitant Prices

There are nine consumer cooperatives in the stadium and dormitory areas, exclusively selling cigarettes, snacks, fruits, and other items. However, the prices are very high. "Sky Bridge" brand cigarettes cost 200 cash per pack, lollipops cost 80 cash each, and fruits and snacks are all marked up by more than 40% compared to usual.大会的職員並不顧問、似乎外來朋友、自應敲上幾個小竹槓也、

▲ Regional Accents

Whenever there is a victory, two thousand athletes gather in the dining hall, feasting heartily and loudly discussing the day's competitions. The Wu dialect and other regional accents vary greatly – some are harsh, some are soft, some are soft yet harsh, and some are harsh with a touch of softness. Coupled with the clatter of bowls and chopsticks, it's like a grand gathering of dialects.

▲ Making a Statement

On the morning of the day before yesterday, the weather was bad, with light rain and unusual cold. The athletes still braved the wind and rain to compete as usual. Male athletes' overcoats and female athletes' large shawls filled the stadium. The Guangdong female athletes' beige leather-collared outerwear was particularly distinctive.

▲ One in Every Hand

Canes made of domestic rattan are a must-have for anyone visiting Hangzhou for strolling. The athletes, finding them cheap and beautiful, bought them en masse and played with them in their hands, appearing quite pleased with themselves.

▲ Skin Injuries

In recent days, many female athletes have been injured from falls during races or have contracted minor illnesses. A survey is as follows: (1) Luo Qiyun of the Zhejiang team (skin abrasion on the knee), (2) Feng Shuzhen of the Jiangxi team (gastritis), (3) Ni Yunmei of the Zhejiang team (skin abrasion on the finger), (4) Liu Jingzhen of Harbin (injuries to upper and lower limbs), (5) Luo Huilin of the Hunan team (sore throat), (6) Zhang Guoqi of the Nanjing team (sunburn on the face), (7) Zhan Zongzeng of the Tianjin team (skin abrasion on the arm), (8) Xu Bang'ai of the Tianjin team (skin abrasion on the arm).

▲ Black and White Distinction

The Guangdong athletes' sportswear consists of white undershirts adorned with red characters indicating "Guangdong." The female athletes are the same, while the lower half consists of long trousers for men and black shorts for women, tightly wrapping around the middle of the thighs. When moving, their inner thighs make fragmented movements.

▲ A Women's Army Parading Through the City

The entire contingent of talents from the Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School has come to Hangzhou to show their mettle. Every day, they proceed in formation from the Lakeside Road area to the stadium, with the military band in the front, the student soldiers in the middle, armed with wooden rifles, and the boy scouts at the rear. Four abreast, about a hundred people in total. The music of the military band is extremely soft, graceful, and nuanced, complemented by the sound of drums, creating a blend of imposingness and gentleness. Each time they pass, the city dwellers stand to watch, and the street urchins call out, "The women's army is here!"

▲ All Hope for Li Huitang

Li Huitang's superb skills are renowned far and wide. Not only do the people of Zhejiang eagerly want to see him, but athletes from all directions also want to take this opportunity to witness Li's great skills. Unfortunately, good things don't last. Li suddenly returned to Shanghai due to illness, which will undoubtedly affect the strength of the Shanghai team. A group of enthusiasts expressed their disappointment.

▲ Zhang Xueliang Introduces Feng Yong

Feng Yong, the principal of Liaoning Feng Yong University, has made outstanding achievements in educational endeavors in the border regions. Since the outbreak of the Middle Eastern Railway issue, which triggered Sino-Russian negotiations, Feng led his student army to Manchuria to resist. He has now come south with his team to experience the flavors of southern China. Zhang Xueliang, in order to comfort a worthy person, sent a telegram to the Games to introduce Feng. It is said that Feng strongly advocates sports and has a particular fondness for basketball and football. Therefore, in recent days, Feng has been a frequent sight in the Games' basketball and football fields.

Brief Biographies of the Athletes 199

▲ Liu Changchun

Liu Changchun is from Jin County, Liaoning Province. He is 21 years old, of magnificent physique, but rather short in stature. He is a top student at Northeastern University. He has no other hobbies in life, except that he is particularly fond of sports. At the age of sixteen, he began to study sports and excelled in everything. Both of his parents are alive and well. After entering the Department of Physical Education at Northeastern University, he specialized in physical education, striving diligently and improving rapidly. He has participated in the North China Games, the Sino-Japanese-German Tripartite Games, and the Sino-Russian Games, winning championships. He has joined the National Games this time, and won first place in the 100-meter and 400-meter races yesterday, truly a prodigy of the Northeast and a leader in sprinting.

▲ Jiang Yunlong

Jiang Yunlong is from Fengcheng County, Liaoning Province. He is 20 years old, strong and robust, but of courteous demeanor. He has studied classical Chinese diligently and has a solid foundation. He is a second-year student in the Department of Classical Chinese at Northeastern University. In his spare time from studying, he likes to engage in outdoor sports, wanting to correct the decadent habits of scholars. He has been studying diligently since the age of sixteen, progressing day by day. He has won championships in the 1500-meter, 5000-meter, and 10,000-meter races at the North China Games. He also ranked first in the individual total score at the Three Eastern Provinces Games, which is truly commendable.

▲ He Zhenkun

▲ First Place in Women's Eight-Pound Shot Put

Ms. He is from Liaoning Province. She is a second-year student at Tongze Women's High School. She is seventeen years old, intelligent, ambitious, and likes to engage in outdoor sports, often saying that Chinese women are often娇弱, how can she shoulder great responsibilities. She was originally in the volleyball and basketball teams, with a reputation for bravery, and she also studied field events with her remaining energy, touching upon everything. This time, she participated in this meeting and won first place in the women's eight-pound bronze ball, which everyone praised as divine. In fact, Ms. He has been engaged in sports for less than two years. Both of Ms. He's parents are currently alive and well, and she is especially loved by them.

▲ Lin Shaoyuan

First Place in Men's High Hurdles

Lin Shaoyuan is from Xiamen County, Fujian Province. He is 20 years old and a first-year student at Jimei School. At the age of eighteen, he began to engage in sports, working hard to improve himself rapidly, so he was able to surpass the crowd and become famous throughout Fujian. Even those who have worked hard for ten years cannot catch up. He is truly a genius. He has won high and low hurdles championships at the Hong Kong Games and this year's Provincial Games. He excels in all outdoor sports, especially ball games. This time, he won the first place championship in the men's high hurdles at this meeting.

▲ Hao Chunde

Hao Chunde is from Panyu, Guangdong Province. He is twelve years old and has been in Shanghai for four or five years. He is in the Department of Psychology at Jinan University, working hard to improve himself. After entering Jinan University, he began to learn sports for less than three years and has achieved remarkable results. He has won the first individual prize at the Jiangnan Games and the Shanghai Open Championship. He also participated in the International Games. This time, he participated in this meeting and won first place in the men's long jump. He is truly an invaluable athlete in our country. Who would say it is not appropriate to call him the pride of sports?

Free Talk

Laughing It Off 202

— Hai Ke

▲ Wife — What is the difference between direct taxation and indirect taxation?

Husband — The difference is very simple. Direct taxation is like you reaching out to me for money every morning. Indirect taxation is like you searching my pockets after I fall asleep every night.

▲ A — I have changed professions now, and I am a new salesman for a furniture store.

B — Have you made any big sales? The commissions must be considerable.

A — I sold a suite of rooms. But I sold it to myself.

▲ Man — Darling, do you know what is closest to my heart in everything?

Woman — Your tie must be the closest to your heart.

▲ A — You borrowed such a large sum of money from me, why don't you write me an IOU?

B — The doctor said I've been overworking my brain. I'm not allowed to write for a year.

▲ A (visiting a Western art exhibition) — Look at the woman in this painting. Lying there naked, white and tender, how lovely.

B — What's the title of the painting?

A — Don't you see the red label on the frame? "Reserved for Mr. Wang."

Anecdotes from the Opening Ceremony of the National Games 203

— Yingchuan Furun, from Hangzhou

The magnificent and enthusiastic National Games had its opening ceremony at West Lake the day before yesterday. More than 20,000 people attended. Having returned from participating in the grand ceremony, the reporter has gathered some anecdotes from the event to share with Juanweng.

The venue was the old military camp, located southeast of Meidong Gaoqiao. The architecture is magnificent, divided into track and field, football, baseball, tennis, and basketball courts, covering an area of about 400 acres. The command platform is located to the west of the field. Several dozen silver cups and shields are displayed in the middle, wondering which athletes will win them. On the platform are Chairman Chiang, his wife Madame Soong Mei-ling, prominent figures of the party and the state such as Dai Jitao, Wang Zhengting, Soong Ziwen, Chu Minyi, Shao Lizi, Chen Guofu, and the Chairman of Zhejiang Province, Zhang Jingjiang, creating a lively scene. Wu Zhihui also attended in plain clothes. His humorous tone during the speech made everyone laugh.

After Chairman Chiang respectfully read Dr. Sun Yat-sen's will, there was a three-minute moment of silence. Although there were as many as 20,000 people in the large venue, it was completely silent. Suddenly, there was a loud cannon sound in the center of the field. Everyone was startled, suspecting it was a bomb. For a moment, the order was disrupted. After inquiries, it was learned that it was the final sound of the twenty-one-gun salute. However, everyone had already experienced a false alarm.

Those who gave speeches included Shao Yuanchong of the Central Party Department and Wang Zhengting of the National Government. Finally, Chairman Chiang gave a speech. To attract the attention of the public, he stood on a trapezoidal platform and used radio waves to broadcast his voice. In addition to calling on the people to pay attention to physical education, Chiang criticized Yan Xishan and Feng Yuxiang of the Northwest for colluding with reactionary elements and endangering the central government. At key points, he gestured with his fist, with a sorrowful and indignant tone, making the entire audience stand in awe.

Fearing that there might be reactionary sabotage, the military and police guards were heavily guarded and prohibited the distribution of any leaflets to curb the source of the chaos. The intention was good. However, while the athletes were standing in a circle to take the oath, the Zhejiang Provincial Executive Committee suddenly distributed five-colored leaflets in the field, with red and green colors fluttering like butterflies, which was very beautiful.

The meeting ended at 11:00 AM. Chairman Chiang and his wife returned to Chiang's Villa in West Lake for dinner. Along the way, reporters scrambled to take pictures, with forty to fifty people surrounding him. Some jokingly said that the Commander-in-Chief was besieged.

A Strange Disease 204

— Ji Jin

In the western countryside of Huzhou, there is an old woman who is nearly sixty years old. Her hair is as black as lacquer and longer than her ankles, surpassing that of young women. One day, she was combing her hair when she was accidentally injured by the teeth of the comb, and blood flowed like a spring. She hurriedly applied medicine to stop it. In the past half month, there have been all kinds of changes, the strangest of which is that if someone touches one of her hairs, her entire body feels pain. When in pain, each strand curls up, and it takes more than an hour to subside.

According to a Western doctor, a woman in Paris once suffered from epilepsy. Whenever it broke out, her hair would stand on end, which was extremely terrifying. This shows that hair on the human body also has nerves and has a sense of feeling. Only those with abundant blood and Qi will not go bald even in old age. The old woman has always been plethoric. Medical treatment is ineffective, and it is feared that she will become insane.

Notes on the Continued Trial of the Gao Ying Case 205

— Zong Yu

Former Vice Consul of San Francisco, Gao Ying, his wife, Ms. Liao, was found to have smuggled luggage for others, which contained opium. The Gao couple was suspected of trafficking opium and was extradited back to China. The Jiangning District Court sentenced them to imprisonment separately. The Gao couple refused to accept the verdict and appealed. Yesterday, the Jiangsu Higher Court held the second trial. I was shaken by the fame of the case, so I went to listen. So I recorded the anecdotes of the meeting, in order to feed my readers.

▲ A Bird's-Eye View of the Venue　The trial began at 2:00 PM yesterday afternoon in the First Tribunal of the court. The court is a large, ancient-style hall in our country. It is extremely spacious. The portrait and will of Dr. Sun Yat-sen are hanging in the middle. There are couplets on the pillars on both sides. The text says: "Rectify the discipline, eliminate the violence and protect the good." The judges' seats are in the middle. Behind it are the seats for the officials to listen. The defendant's seat is in the front. The lawyers' seats are in the center of the court. The journalists' seats are on both sides. The audience seats are behind the lawyers' seats. The layout is very neat. Although there were three or four hundred listeners, they remained silent throughout. It was really solemn.

▲ Difficult to Obtain Audience Tickets　In view of the congestion at the first trial of the case, the court issued audience tickets this time, with strict restrictions. All those who requested tickets had to be introduced by agencies or groups with letters. The court's publicity office was dedicated to this matter. Therefore, hundreds of people were denied entry. The audience members were mostly representatives and staff from various agencies and academia. Women accounted for four out of ten of the total number, which also shows the general attention of women to the rule of law.

▲ Liao, the Blackened Gao's Wife　Ms. Gao wore a full body of black clothing, except for her jade-colored stockings. Her curly hair was fluffy, covering her cheeks, and she was wrapped in a Yuan-colored thin veil embroidered with black flowers. The veil hung down her back. She wore a black Indian silk cheongsam and black velvet high-heeled shoes. She was plump, but her face was sallow and her expression depressed. She was very different from her old self.

▲ Two Foreign Firm Runners　Gao Ying and Sun Yuan both wore small-legged Western-style pants and Chinese-style cotton robes that were only knee-length, much like foreign firm runners. However, Gao's blue foreign cloth robe and black straight tribute ne shoes were far less beautiful than Sun's silk robe and leather shoes. Sun Yuan's demeanor was still natural, while Gao was drooping his head, looking very painful. Onlookers, thinking that his talent could be used, could not help but feel sorry for him.

▲ Lawyer Liu Surrounded by People　Although the case was being heard for the second time, due to the complexity of the case, the facts were still being examined yesterday and there was no debate. The lawyer had no chance to speak throughout. After the court adjourned, reporters from various newspapers flocked to Gao Ying's defense lawyer, Liu Shifang, to inquire about his opinions and arguments on the case. Lawyer Liu politely declined, saying that it was not yet time to publish. He hurriedly returned to the lawyer's lounge. The reporters still surrounded him and asked questions without dispersing. Lawyer Liu then handed over the old San Francisco lawyer Wahl Lai who testified in court to prove that Consul General Gong disagreed with Gao Ying and other letters that could be used as evidence, and gave them to the reporters to copy.

▲ Eyeglasses Exhibition　Most of the viewers on this day wore eyeglasses. All kinds of Roque-style flat-edged mirrors, non-sleepy style, and old-fashioned copper-edged straight-leg styles were available. New and old were all available, and everything was beautiful. Some of the viewers raised their heads and listened quietly, and some jokingly said that they were opening an eyeglasses exhibition that could be compared with the Shanghai fashion exhibition.

A Record of Walking to Beijing (Part II) 206

— Liu Hanru, Member of the National Walking Group

On March 2nd, we went to Changshu. We encountered rain in Changshu for days, which made it impossible to move forward. We were treated to everything by the Changshu Branch of the China National Road Construction Association. The news industry in Changshu is extremely developed. There are as many as twelve newspaper offices in the whole city. For example, the Qinbao is larger, with a daily circulation of 1,500 copies. It is rare to see more than ten newspaper offices in a small county town. On the 8th, we were guided by Cheng Junjunyan, the general manager of the branch, to tour Yushan. We did not leave Changshu until the afternoon of the 10th to go to Wuxi. On the evening of the 10th, we stayed at the home of Bao Jun in Wangzhuang, on the border between Changshu and Wuxi. The next morning, we encountered rain after walking about ten li. We continued to move forward in the rain. The rain became heavier and heavier, and the raincoats lost their effectiveness. In addition, the road was muddy, and we slipped at every step. Comrade Xu fell four times in a row, which made us feel that we could not move forward. At 6:00 PM, we arrived in Wuxi. Our clothes were wet inside and out, like a drowned chicken. We stayed in Wuxi for several days, visiting various factories and touring Huishan and Meiyuan. On the 15th, we left Wuxi for Changzhou. We visited Qian Mingshan (Zhenhuang), a famous scholar in Jiangnan, in Changzhou. On the afternoon of the 16th, we left Changzhou for Danyang. That night, we stayed overnight in Xinzha Town in the county. The villagers were closing their doors. Because it was not yet dark, there was no reason to go to bed. Later, Liu, the platoon leader of the garrison, came and told us that some villagers had reported to him that six bandits had arrived in the town, so they all closed their doors. We told them about our mission. Liu explained to the villagers, and they all calmed down. Fortunately, Liu did not trade in his business, otherwise he would have led his troops to fire guns. We also suspected that the bandits were robbing, which would have been a terrible misunderstanding. We set off at 5:00 AM on the 17th and arrived in Danyang City at 6:00 PM. We stayed in Danyang for a day. On the evening of the 18th, we camped out at Zhaize Station, ten li away from Zhenjiang. We arrived in Zhenjiang at dawn on the 19th. It was the reorganization of the provincial government. The Zhenjiang column of a certain newspaper reported that our group had arrived in Zhenjiang by car, which was not accurate. On the 24th, we left Zhenjiang for Beijing. We stayed overnight at the Longtan Cement Factory. We arrived in Beijing on the evening of the 25th. We entered Taipingmen. President Zheng Shaojue of Jinan University specially opened the Jinan University Alumni Association as our residence. This is a brief record of our journey from Shanghai to Ningbo.

It took us thirty-three days to reach Beijing this time. On average, we walked more than sixty li a day. There are about 1,400 steps per kilometer. Some villagers said that we were measuring the railway, and some said that we were doing business. There were various rumors. In terms of accommodation, we either slept on copper beds, or lay on the grass, or ate mountain delicacies, or ate Rao cakes. The environment changed every day. Our bodies felt a little pain, but our spirits increased greatly. There was endless fun. We obtained documents from the official office for reference and confirmed them to the people along the way. We plan to stay in Beijing for ten days and then cross the canal to the north. We hope that the advanced people in Shanghai will give us more instructions to correct our deficiencies.

A Record of Guan Gong Crab 207

— Sang Junfu

My hometown, Shangyu, has beautiful mountains and rivers and natural scenery. It is located in the Qiantang River tributary, and the most beautiful place is Xihua Village, about forty li away from the West Gate. There is a swamp called Shuanglian Lotus Pond, which is also a scenic spot. According to legend, the pond was formed by a tidal surge during the Song Dynasty. When Liang Shanbo was the county magistrate of Shangyu, he often led his subordinates to fish there during the summer. The pond is not very deep, but the area is very wide, and the silt is very thick. Lotuses are planted all over the pond. Every Midsummer, when the lotus blossoms are in full bloom, the fragrance of lotuses can be smelled for ten li. Recently, a kind of crustacean has suddenly appeared in the pond. It is similar to a crab but slightly smaller. The color of the back shell is slightly red, similar to the color of shrimp shells after being cooked, and the patterns are shaped like ears, eyes, mouth, and nose, forming a spectacle. The villagers who saw it were amazed. According to old fishermen in central Zhejiang, this kind of crustacean is called Guan Gong Crab. In the past, a small number of them were found in Jinhua, Quzhou, Yan, and other places in southern Zhejiang, but now they have disappeared. It is said that the emergence of this crab is due to the blood of Guan Gong flowing into the water after he was killed. I think this statement is similar to the Qi Dong Ye Yu and is not enough to be a sign. However, the emergence of this crustacean is really strange. Therefore, I recorded it for the research of naturalists.

Warmth in the Heart ㈠㈥㈢ 209

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 10 Filial Piety from the Curtain. Meeting the Famous Players

At this time. Inside the Tsingliu Society, there was one most cheerful person. This person's surname was Lu, and his name was Lu Junfu. He was from Changzhou, and he had studied in Japan for many years. He also married a Japanese woman. Originally, China and Japan were of the same race and culture after all, so many Japanese women liked to marry Chinese men. In terms of physique, Chinese men were tall and upright, unlike the short and stout Japanese. Especially like Lu Junfu, standing in the middle of Japanese men, he looked even more like a crane standing among chickens. He was originally a tall man. There was another reason why Japanese women were willing to marry Chinese. It was that Japanese women were very bitter. They took serving men as their heavenly duty. In reality, Japanese men and women were the most unequal. In middle-class families, they could not hire servants, so they had to do everything themselves. Even barefoot, scrubbing the floor and so on, they had to do it themselves. In China, even middle-class families hired an old nanny or a young maid. Women could call themselves Madame at any time. After eating their fill, they could do nothing, or play mahjong to pass the time. Therefore, after a few women who had married Chinese said so, when they saw how carefree it was, they could not help but envy them. Therefore, at that time, many Japanese women were willing to marry Chinese students. Lu Junfu was also a member of the Tsingliu Society. He played a young man in the new drama. He was the most suave and refined. Before the premiere, he was the most active. The script they chose was called "Hototogisu". This "Hototogisu" was originally a famous Japanese novel. It was written by a Japanese novelist, Tokutomi Roka. This novel caused quite a stir when it came out. Almost everyone had one copy. Even Europeans translated it into Western languages. In Japan, it was adapted into a script and performed several times in theaters. When they were studying in Japan, they naturally went to see it. Later, their Tsingliu Society also performed it once or twice. When the Japanese performed it, they used Japanese. When the Chinese performed it, of course, they used Chinese. Fortunately, their dramas had scripts that were made public. As long as you bought their scripts and studied them, and Japanese performers were also scholars, unlike the so-called Chinese actors, some of whom did not even know the characters, but were a bunch of rude people. Therefore, when they performed that "Hototogisu" in Japan, they asked them to guide them, and they were all happy to do so. This "Hototogisu" was a family tragedy. It described a woman who married a husband. They were very affectionate. Unexpectedly, her mother-in-law was very fierce. Because the daughter-in-law had lung disease, she drove her out when her son went to the military. The woman's lung disease was very deep. After this blow, she died in her mother's home. Her mother was a stepmother. Later, until she died, she did not see her husband. When the husband received the news of her death, he himself was injured in a field hospital.

New Voices for Opening Silk Cocoon Loans 214

This year, the financial community is particularly cautious about various loan businesses due to market conditions. Therefore, everyone is hesitant to contact and negotiate early for silk cocoon loans. General silk foreign firms and silk merchants have tried their best to raise money, but to no avail, resulting in a dull atmosphere in the silk cocoon market. It is vaguely heard that the money shops have not yet expressed their approval or disapproval of the trading of these 37 silk cocoon loans, so there has been no transaction. However, some Chinese commercial banks have already been in contact. According to investigations, Zhejiang silk merchants have agreed to about 300,000 to 400,000, with unspecified interest rates. Jiangsu silk merchants have agreed to 700,000 to 800,000, with interest rates of 9 taels and a half to 10 taels, with a term of two to three months, and repayment at any time. Other silk merchants and foreign firms with various stocks and actual assets still have old accounts to pad the loans, which are not examples of doing business. All the selling period foreign exchange rates have not been opened, only agreeing to use a certain amount of tens of thousands, and when it is time to use it, settling the price according to the foreign exchange rate on that day, so that both parties do not suffer losses. From now on, the transaction of period foreign exchange rates will be completely eliminated.

Yarn and Cotton - Spot Yarn Slightly Better, Sales Still Flat 216

▲ Suspension of Auction for Future Yarn... Foreign Firms Reluctant to Exert Effort

The Yarn Market is Slightly Better, and American Cotton Has Risen Again, Stabilizing People's Sentiment. News from the Publishing World 226

▲ **A Prelude to Standardizing the Translation of Engineering Terminology:** The Chinese Institute of Engineers Declares - Our country's translation of Western academic masterpieces on European and American subjects has resulted in each translator issuing their own opinions regarding specialized terminology. There is a complete lack of standards, causing readers to waste time understanding. This is hardly the way to promote academics. In view of this, the Institute established the Engineering Terminology Compilation Committee to translate engineering terms from various countries, hoping to standardize the translation of engineering terms. The Committee has already translated seven drafts of English engineering terms and published them to solicit opinions from experts nationwide. The rest are still being compiled and selected with continued effort. The types and prices are as follows: Draft of Electrical Engineering Terms, 30 cents per copy; Draft of Civil, Mechanical, Chemical Engineering Terms, 20 cents per copy; Draft of Aviation, Dyeing, Radio Engineering Terms, 10 cents per copy. The sales location is the Institute's office at 7 Ningbo Road. The Institute also plans to proceed with the work of compiling engineering symbols.
